stm32f1xx_hal_i2c.c
Go to the documentation of this file.
00001 /**
00002   ******************************************************************************
00003   * @file    stm32f1xx_hal_i2c.c
00004   * @author  MCD Application Team
00005   * @brief   I2C HAL module driver.
00006   *          This file provides firmware functions to manage the following
00007   *          functionalities of the Inter Integrated Circuit (I2C) peripheral:
00008   *           + Initialization and de-initialization functions
00009   *           + IO operation functions
00010   *           + Peripheral State, Mode and Error functions
00011   *
00012   @verbatim
00013   ==============================================================================
00014                         ##### How to use this driver #####
00015   ==============================================================================
00016   [..]
00017     The I2C HAL driver can be used as follows:
00018 
00019     (#) Declare a I2C_HandleTypeDef handle structure, for example:
00020         I2C_HandleTypeDef  hi2c;
00021 
00022     (#)Initialize the I2C low level resources by implementing the @ref HAL_I2C_MspInit() API:
00023         (##) Enable the I2Cx interface clock
00024         (##) I2C pins configuration
00025             (+++) Enable the clock for the I2C GPIOs
00026             (+++) Configure I2C pins as alternate function open-drain
00027         (##) NVIC configuration if you need to use interrupt process
00028             (+++) Configure the I2Cx interrupt priority
00029             (+++) Enable the NVIC I2C IRQ Channel
00030         (##) DMA Configuration if you need to use DMA process
00031             (+++) Declare a DMA_HandleTypeDef handle structure for the transmit or receive channel
00032             (+++) Enable the DMAx interface clock using
00033             (+++) Configure the DMA handle parameters
00034             (+++) Configure the DMA Tx or Rx channel
00035             (+++) Associate the initialized DMA handle to the hi2c DMA Tx or Rx handle
00036             (+++) Configure the priority and enable the NVIC for the transfer complete interrupt on
00037                   the DMA Tx or Rx channel
00038 
00039     (#) Configure the Communication Speed, Duty cycle, Addressing mode, Own Address1,
00040         Dual Addressing mode, Own Address2, General call and Nostretch mode in the hi2c Init structure.
00041 
00042     (#) Initialize the I2C registers by calling the @ref HAL_I2C_Init(), configures also the low level Hardware
00043         (GPIO, CLOCK, NVIC...etc) by calling the customized @ref HAL_I2C_MspInit() API.
00044 
00045     (#) To check if target device is ready for communication, use the function @ref HAL_I2C_IsDeviceReady()
00046 
00047     (#) For I2C IO and IO MEM operations, three operation modes are available within this driver :
00048 
00049     *** Polling mode IO operation ***
00050     =================================
00051     [..]
00052       (+) Transmit in master mode an amount of data in blocking mode using @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Transmit()
00053       (+) Receive in master mode an amount of data in blocking mode using @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Receive()
00054       (+) Transmit in slave mode an amount of data in blocking mode using @ref HAL_I2C_Slave_Transmit()
00055       (+) Receive in slave mode an amount of data in blocking mode using @ref HAL_I2C_Slave_Receive()
00056 
00057     *** Polling mode IO MEM operation ***
00058     =====================================
00059     [..]
00060       (+) Write an amount of data in blocking mode to a specific memory address using @ref HAL_I2C_Mem_Write()
00061       (+) Read an amount of data in blocking mode from a specific memory address using @ref HAL_I2C_Mem_Read()
00062 
00063 
00064     *** Interrupt mode IO operation ***
00065     ===================================
00066     [..]
00067       (+) Transmit in master mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode using @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Transmit_IT()
00068       (+) At transmission end of transfer, @ref HAL_I2C_MasterTxCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00069            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_MasterTxCpltCallback()
00070       (+) Receive in master mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode using @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Receive_IT()
00071       (+) At reception end of transfer, @ref HAL_I2C_MasterRxCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00072            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_MasterRxCpltCallback()
00073       (+) Transmit in slave mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode using @ref HAL_I2C_Slave_Transmit_IT()
00074       (+) At transmission end of transfer, @ref HAL_I2C_SlaveTxCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00075            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_SlaveTxCpltCallback()
00076       (+) Receive in slave mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode using @ref HAL_I2C_Slave_Receive_IT()
00077       (+) At reception end of transfer, @ref HAL_I2C_SlaveRxCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00078            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_SlaveRxCpltCallback()
00079       (+) In case of transfer Error, @ref HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback() function is executed and user can
00080            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback()
00081       (+) Abort a master I2C process communication with Interrupt using @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Abort_IT()
00082       (+) End of abort process, @ref HAL_I2C_AbortCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00083            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_AbortCpltCallback()
00084 
00085     *** Interrupt mode or DMA mode IO sequential operation ***
00086     ==========================================================
00087     [..]
00088       (@) These interfaces allow to manage a sequential transfer with a repeated start condition
00089           when a direction change during transfer
00090     [..]
00091       (+) A specific option field manage the different steps of a sequential transfer
00092       (+) Option field values are defined through @ref I2C_XferOptions_definition and are listed below:
00093       (++) I2C_FIRST_AND_LAST_FRAME: No sequential usage, functionnal is same as associated interfaces in no sequential mode
00094       (++) I2C_FIRST_FRAME: Sequential usage, this option allow to manage a sequence with start condition, address
00095                             and data to transfer without a final stop condition
00096       (++) I2C_FIRST_AND_NEXT_FRAME: Sequential usage (Master only), this option allow to manage a sequence with start condition, address
00097                             and data to transfer without a final stop condition, an then permit a call the same master sequential interface
00098                             several times (like @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Transmit_IT() then @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Transmit_IT()
00099                             or @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Transmit_DMA() then @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Transmit_DMA())
00100       (++) I2C_NEXT_FRAME: Sequential usage, this option allow to manage a sequence with a restart condition, address
00101                             and with new data to transfer if the direction change or manage only the new data to transfer
00102                             if no direction change and without a final stop condition in both cases
00103       (++) I2C_LAST_FRAME: Sequential usage, this option allow to manage a sequance with a restart condition, address
00104                             and with new data to transfer if the direction change or manage only the new data to transfer
00105                             if no direction change and with a final stop condition in both cases
00106       (++) I2C_LAST_FRAME_NO_STOP: Sequential usage (Master only), this option allow to manage a restart condition after several call of the same master sequential
00107                             interface several times (link with option I2C_FIRST_AND_NEXT_FRAME).
00108                             Usage can, transfer several bytes one by one using HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Transmit_IT(option I2C_FIRST_AND_NEXT_FRAME then I2C_NEXT_FRAME)
00109                               or HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Receive_IT(option I2C_FIRST_AND_NEXT_FRAME then I2C_NEXT_FRAME)
00110                               or HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Transmit_DMA(option I2C_FIRST_AND_NEXT_FRAME then I2C_NEXT_FRAME)
00111                               or HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Receive_DMA(option I2C_FIRST_AND_NEXT_FRAME then I2C_NEXT_FRAME).
00112                             Then usage of this option I2C_LAST_FRAME_NO_STOP at the last Transmit or Receive sequence permit to call the oposite interface Receive or Transmit
00113                               without stopping the communication and so generate a restart condition.
00114       (++) I2C_OTHER_FRAME: Sequential usage (Master only), this option allow to manage a restart condition after each call of the same master sequential
00115                             interface.
00116                             Usage can, transfer several bytes one by one with a restart with slave address between each bytes using HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Transmit_IT(option I2C_FIRST_FRAME then I2C_OTHER_FRAME)
00117                               or HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Receive_IT(option I2C_FIRST_FRAME then I2C_OTHER_FRAME)
00118                               or HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Transmit_DMA(option I2C_FIRST_FRAME then I2C_OTHER_FRAME)
00119                               or HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Receive_DMA(option I2C_FIRST_FRAME then I2C_OTHER_FRAME).
00120                             Then usage of this option I2C_OTHER_AND_LAST_FRAME at the last frame to help automatic generation of STOP condition.
00121 
00122       (+) Differents sequential I2C interfaces are listed below:
00123       (++) Sequential transmit in master I2C mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode using @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Transmit_IT()
00124             or using @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Transmit_DMA()
00125       (+++) At transmission end of current frame transfer, @ref HAL_I2C_MasterTxCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00126            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_MasterTxCpltCallback()
00127       (++) Sequential receive in master I2C mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode using @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Receive_IT()
00128             or using @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Receive_DMA()
00129       (+++) At reception end of current frame transfer, @ref HAL_I2C_MasterRxCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00130            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_MasterRxCpltCallback()
00131       (++) Abort a master IT or DMA I2C process communication with Interrupt using @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Abort_IT()
00132       (+++) End of abort process, @ref HAL_I2C_AbortCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00133            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_AbortCpltCallback()
00134       (++) Enable/disable the Address listen mode in slave I2C mode using @ref HAL_I2C_EnableListen_IT() @ref HAL_I2C_DisableListen_IT()
00135       (+++) When address slave I2C match, @ref HAL_I2C_AddrCallback() is executed and user can
00136            add his own code to check the Address Match Code and the transmission direction request by master (Write/Read).
00137       (+++) At Listen mode end @ref HAL_I2C_ListenCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00138            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_ListenCpltCallback()
00139       (++) Sequential transmit in slave I2C mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode using @ref HAL_I2C_Slave_Seq_Transmit_IT()
00140             or using @ref HAL_I2C_Slave_Seq_Transmit_DMA()
00141       (+++) At transmission end of current frame transfer, @ref HAL_I2C_SlaveTxCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00142            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_SlaveTxCpltCallback()
00143       (++) Sequential receive in slave I2C mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode using @ref HAL_I2C_Slave_Seq_Receive_IT()
00144             or using @ref HAL_I2C_Slave_Seq_Receive_DMA()
00145       (+++) At reception end of current frame transfer, @ref HAL_I2C_SlaveRxCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00146            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_SlaveRxCpltCallback()
00147       (++) In case of transfer Error, @ref HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback() function is executed and user can
00148            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback()
00149 
00150     *** Interrupt mode IO MEM operation ***
00151     =======================================
00152     [..]
00153       (+) Write an amount of data in non-blocking mode with Interrupt to a specific memory address using
00154           @ref HAL_I2C_Mem_Write_IT()
00155       (+) At Memory end of write transfer, @ref HAL_I2C_MemTxCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00156            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_MemTxCpltCallback()
00157       (+) Read an amount of data in non-blocking mode with Interrupt from a specific memory address using
00158           @ref HAL_I2C_Mem_Read_IT()
00159       (+) At Memory end of read transfer, @ref HAL_I2C_MemRxCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00160            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_MemRxCpltCallback()
00161       (+) In case of transfer Error, @ref HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback() function is executed and user can
00162            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback()
00163 
00164     *** DMA mode IO operation ***
00165     ==============================
00166     [..]
00167       (+) Transmit in master mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode (DMA) using
00168           @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Transmit_DMA()
00169       (+) At transmission end of transfer, @ref HAL_I2C_MasterTxCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00170            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_MasterTxCpltCallback()
00171       (+) Receive in master mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode (DMA) using
00172           @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Receive_DMA()
00173       (+) At reception end of transfer, @ref HAL_I2C_MasterRxCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00174            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_MasterRxCpltCallback()
00175       (+) Transmit in slave mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode (DMA) using
00176           @ref HAL_I2C_Slave_Transmit_DMA()
00177       (+) At transmission end of transfer, @ref HAL_I2C_SlaveTxCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00178            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_SlaveTxCpltCallback()
00179       (+) Receive in slave mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode (DMA) using
00180           @ref HAL_I2C_Slave_Receive_DMA()
00181       (+) At reception end of transfer, @ref HAL_I2C_SlaveRxCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00182            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_SlaveRxCpltCallback()
00183       (+) In case of transfer Error, @ref HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback() function is executed and user can
00184            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback()
00185       (+) Abort a master I2C process communication with Interrupt using @ref HAL_I2C_Master_Abort_IT()
00186       (+) End of abort process, @ref HAL_I2C_AbortCpltCallback() is executed and user can
00187            add his own code by customization of function pointer @ref HAL_I2C_AbortCpltCallback()
00188 
00189     *** DMA mode IO MEM operation ***
00190     =================================
00191     [..]
00192       (+) Write an amount of data in non-blocking mode with DMA to a specific memory address using

00194       (+) At Memory end of write transfer, @ref HAL_I2C_MemTxCpltCallback() is executed and user can

00203 
00204      *** I2C HAL driver macros list ***
00205      ==================================
00206      [..]
00207        Below the list of most used macros in I2C HAL driver.
00208 
00209       (+) @ref __HAL_I2C_ENABLE:     Enable the I2C peripheral
00210       (+) @ref __HAL_I2C_DISABLE:    Disable the I2C peripheral
00211       (+) @ref __HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG:   Checks whether the specified I2C flag is set or not
00212       (+) @ref __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_FLAG: Clear the specified I2C pending flag
00213       (+) @ref __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT:  Enable the specified I2C interrupt
00214       (+) @ref __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT: Disable the specified I2C interrupt
00215 
00216      *** Callback registration ***
00217      =============================================
00218 
00219      The compilation flag USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS when set to 1
00220      allows the user to configure dynamically the driver callbacks.
00221      Use Functions @ref HAL_I2C_RegisterCallback() or @ref HAL_I2C_RegisterAddrCallback()
00222      to register an interrupt callback.
00223 
00224      Function @ref HAL_I2C_RegisterCallback() allows to register following callbacks:
00225        (+) MasterTxCpltCallback : callback for Master transmission end of transfer.
00226        (+) MasterRxCpltCallback : callback for Master reception end of transfer.
00227        (+) SlaveTxCpltCallback  : callback for Slave transmission end of transfer.
00228        (+) SlaveRxCpltCallback  : callback for Slave reception end of transfer.
00229        (+) ListenCpltCallback   : callback for end of listen mode.
00230        (+) MemTxCpltCallback    : callback for Memory transmission end of transfer.
00231        (+) MemRxCpltCallback    : callback for Memory reception end of transfer.
00232        (+) ErrorCallback        : callback for error detection.
00233        (+) AbortCpltCallback    : callback for abort completion process.
00234        (+) MspInitCallback      : callback for Msp Init.
00235        (+) MspDeInitCallback    : callback for Msp DeInit.
00236      This function takes as parameters the HAL peripheral handle, the Callback ID
00237      and a pointer to the user callback function.
00238 
00239      For specific callback AddrCallback use dedicated register callbacks : @ref HAL_I2C_RegisterAddrCallback().
00240 
00241      Use function @ref HAL_I2C_UnRegisterCallback to reset a callback to the default
00242      weak function.
00243      @ref HAL_I2C_UnRegisterCallback takes as parameters the HAL peripheral handle,
00244      and the Callback ID.
00245      This function allows to reset following callbacks:
00246        (+) MasterTxCpltCallback : callback for Master transmission end of transfer.
00247        (+) MasterRxCpltCallback : callback for Master reception end of transfer.
00248        (+) SlaveTxCpltCallback  : callback for Slave transmission end of transfer.
00249        (+) SlaveRxCpltCallback  : callback for Slave reception end of transfer.
00250        (+) ListenCpltCallback   : callback for end of listen mode.
00251        (+) MemTxCpltCallback    : callback for Memory transmission end of transfer.
00252        (+) MemRxCpltCallback    : callback for Memory reception end of transfer.
00253        (+) ErrorCallback        : callback for error detection.
00254        (+) AbortCpltCallback    : callback for abort completion process.
00255        (+) MspInitCallback      : callback for Msp Init.
00256        (+) MspDeInitCallback    : callback for Msp DeInit.
00257 
00258      For callback AddrCallback use dedicated register callbacks : @ref HAL_I2C_UnRegisterAddrCallback().
00259 
00260      By default, after the @ref HAL_I2C_Init() and when the state is @ref HAL_I2C_STATE_RESET
00261      all callbacks are set to the corresponding weak functions:
00262      examples @ref HAL_I2C_MasterTxCpltCallback(), @ref HAL_I2C_MasterRxCpltCallback().
00263      Exception done for MspInit and MspDeInit functions that are
00264      reset to the legacy weak functions in the @ref HAL_I2C_Init()/ @ref HAL_I2C_DeInit() only when
00265      these callbacks are null (not registered beforehand).
00266      If MspInit or MspDeInit are not null, the @ref HAL_I2C_Init()/ @ref HAL_I2C_DeInit()
00267      keep and use the user MspInit/MspDeInit callbacks (registered beforehand) whatever the state.
00268 
00269      Callbacks can be registered/unregistered in @ref HAL_I2C_STATE_READY state only.
00270      Exception done MspInit/MspDeInit functions that can be registered/unregistered
00271      in @ref HAL_I2C_STATE_READY or @ref HAL_I2C_STATE_RESET state,
00272      thus registered (user) MspInit/DeInit callbacks can be used during the Init/DeInit.
00273      Then, the user first registers the MspInit/MspDeInit user callbacks
00274      using @ref HAL_I2C_RegisterCallback() before calling @ref HAL_I2C_DeInit()
00275      or @ref HAL_I2C_Init() function.
00276 
00277      When the compilation flag USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS is set to 0 or
00278      not defined, the callback registration feature is not available and all callbacks
00279      are set to the corresponding weak functions.
00280 
00281 
00282      *** I2C Workarounds linked to Silicon Limitation ***
00283      ====================================================
00284      [..]
00285        Below the list of all silicon limitations implemented for HAL on STM32F1xx product.
00286        (@) See ErrataSheet to know full silicon limitation list of your product.
00287 
00288        (+) Workarounds Implemented inside I2C HAL Driver
00289           (++) Wrong data read into data register (Polling and Interrupt mode)
00290           (++) Start cannot be generated after a misplaced Stop
00291           (++) Some software events must be managed before the current byte is being transferred:
00292                Workaround: Use DMA in general, except when the Master is receiving a single byte.
00293                For Interupt mode, I2C should have the highest priority in the application.
00294           (++) Mismatch on the "Setup time for a repeated Start condition" timing parameter:
00295                Workaround: Reduce the frequency down to 88 kHz or use the I2C Fast-mode if
00296                supported by the slave.
00297           (++) Data valid time (tVD;DAT) violated without the OVR flag being set:
00298                Workaround: If the slave device allows it, use the clock stretching mechanism
00299                by programming NoStretchMode = I2C_NOSTRETCH_DISABLE in @ref HAL_I2C_Init.
00300 
00301      [..]
00302        (@) You can refer to the I2C HAL driver header file for more useful macros
00303

00343 #define I2C_STATE_MSK             ((uint32_t)((uint32_t)((uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX | (uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX) & (uint32_t)(~((uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)))) /*!< Mask State define, keep only RX and TX bits            */

00347 #define I2C_STATE_SLAVE_BUSY_TX   ((uint32_t)(((uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX & I2C_STATE_MSK) | (uint32_t)HAL_I2C_MODE_SLAVE))             /*!< Slave Busy TX, combinaison of State LSB and Mode enum  */

00379 static HAL_StatusTypeDef I2C_WaitOnSTOPFlagUntilTimeout(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint32_t Timeout, uint32_t Tickstart);
00380 static HAL_StatusTypeDef I2C_IsAcknowledgeFailed(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c);

00411 /** @defgroup I2C_Exported_Functions_Group1 Initialization and de-initialization functions
00412  *  @brief    Initialization and Configuration functions
00413  *
00414 @verbatim
00415  ===============================================================================
00416               ##### Initialization and de-initialization functions #####
00417  ===============================================================================
00418     [..]  This subsection provides a set of functions allowing to initialize and
00419           deinitialize the I2Cx peripheral:
00420 
00421       (+) User must Implement HAL_I2C_MspInit() function in which he configures
00422           all related peripherals resources (CLOCK, GPIO, DMA, IT and NVIC).
00423 
00424       (+) Call the function HAL_I2C_Init() to configure the selected device with
00425           the selected configuration:
00426         (++) Communication Speed
00427         (++) Duty cycle
00428         (++) Addressing mode
00429         (++) Own Address 1
00430         (++) Dual Addressing mode
00431         (++) Own Address 2
00432         (++) General call mode
00433         (++) Nostretch mode
00434 
00435       (+) Call the function HAL_I2C_DeInit() to restore the default configuration
00436           of the selected I2Cx peripheral.
00437 
00438 @endverbatim
00439   * @{
00440   */
00441 
00442 /**
00443   * @brief  Initializes the I2C according to the specified parameters
00444   *         in the I2C_InitTypeDef and initialize the associated handle.
00445   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
00446   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
00447   * @retval HAL status
00448   */
00449 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Init(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
00450 {
00451   uint32_t freqrange;
00452   uint32_t pclk1;
00453 
00454   /* Check the I2C handle allocation */
00455   if (hi2c == NULL)
00456   {
00457     return HAL_ERROR;
00458   }
00459 
00460   /* Check the parameters */
00461   assert_param(IS_I2C_ALL_INSTANCE(hi2c->Instance));
00462   assert_param(IS_I2C_CLOCK_SPEED(hi2c->Init.ClockSpeed));
00463   assert_param(IS_I2C_DUTY_CYCLE(hi2c->Init.DutyCycle));
00464   assert_param(IS_I2C_OWN_ADDRESS1(hi2c->Init.OwnAddress1));
00465   assert_param(IS_I2C_ADDRESSING_MODE(hi2c->Init.AddressingMode));
00466   assert_param(IS_I2C_DUAL_ADDRESS(hi2c->Init.DualAddressMode));
00467   assert_param(IS_I2C_OWN_ADDRESS2(hi2c->Init.OwnAddress2));
00468   assert_param(IS_I2C_GENERAL_CALL(hi2c->Init.GeneralCallMode));
00469   assert_param(IS_I2C_NO_STRETCH(hi2c->Init.NoStretchMode));
00470 
00471   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_RESET)
00472   {
00473     /* Allocate lock resource and initialize it */
00474     hi2c->Lock = HAL_UNLOCKED;
00475 
00476 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
00477     /* Init the I2C Callback settings */
00478     hi2c->MasterTxCpltCallback = HAL_I2C_MasterTxCpltCallback; /* Legacy weak MasterTxCpltCallback */
00479     hi2c->MasterRxCpltCallback = HAL_I2C_MasterRxCpltCallback; /* Legacy weak MasterRxCpltCallback */
00480     hi2c->SlaveTxCpltCallback  = HAL_I2C_SlaveTxCpltCallback;  /* Legacy weak SlaveTxCpltCallback  */
00481     hi2c->SlaveRxCpltCallback  = HAL_I2C_SlaveRxCpltCallback;  /* Legacy weak SlaveRxCpltCallback  */
00482     hi2c->ListenCpltCallback   = HAL_I2C_ListenCpltCallback;   /* Legacy weak ListenCpltCallback   */
00483     hi2c->MemTxCpltCallback    = HAL_I2C_MemTxCpltCallback;    /* Legacy weak MemTxCpltCallback    */
00484     hi2c->MemRxCpltCallback    = HAL_I2C_MemRxCpltCallback;    /* Legacy weak MemRxCpltCallback    */
00485     hi2c->ErrorCallback        = HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback;        /* Legacy weak ErrorCallback        */
00486     hi2c->AbortCpltCallback    = HAL_I2C_AbortCpltCallback;    /* Legacy weak AbortCpltCallback    */
00487     hi2c->AddrCallback         = HAL_I2C_AddrCallback;         /* Legacy weak AddrCallback         */
00488 
00489     if (hi2c->MspInitCallback == NULL)
00490     {
00491       hi2c->MspInitCallback = HAL_I2C_MspInit; /* Legacy weak MspInit  */
00492     }
00493 
00494     /* Init the low level hardware : GPIO, CLOCK, NVIC */
00495     hi2c->MspInitCallback(hi2c);
00496 #else
00497     /* Init the low level hardware : GPIO, CLOCK, NVIC */
00498     HAL_I2C_MspInit(hi2c);
00499 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
00500   }
00501 
00502   hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY;
00503 
00504   /* Disable the selected I2C peripheral */
00505   __HAL_I2C_DISABLE(hi2c);
00506 
00507   /* Get PCLK1 frequency */
00508   pclk1 = HAL_RCC_GetPCLK1Freq();
00509 
00510   /* Check the minimum allowed PCLK1 frequency */
00511   if (I2C_MIN_PCLK_FREQ(pclk1, hi2c->Init.ClockSpeed) == 1U)
00512   {
00513     return HAL_ERROR;
00514   }
00515 
00516   /* Calculate frequency range */
00517   freqrange = I2C_FREQRANGE(pclk1);
00518 
00519   /*---------------------------- I2Cx CR2 Configuration ----------------------*/
00520   /* Configure I2Cx: Frequency range */
00521   MODIFY_REG(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_FREQ, freqrange);
00522 
00523   /*---------------------------- I2Cx TRISE Configuration --------------------*/
00524   /* Configure I2Cx: Rise Time */
00525   MODIFY_REG(hi2c->Instance->TRISE, I2C_TRISE_TRISE, I2C_RISE_TIME(freqrange, hi2c->Init.ClockSpeed));
00526 
00527   /*---------------------------- I2Cx CCR Configuration ----------------------*/
00528   /* Configure I2Cx: Speed */
00529   MODIFY_REG(hi2c->Instance->CCR, (I2C_CCR_FS | I2C_CCR_DUTY | I2C_CCR_CCR), I2C_SPEED(pclk1, hi2c->Init.ClockSpeed, hi2c->Init.DutyCycle));
00530 
00531   /*---------------------------- I2Cx CR1 Configuration ----------------------*/
00532   /* Configure I2Cx: Generalcall and NoStretch mode */
00533   MODIFY_REG(hi2c->Instance->CR1, (I2C_CR1_ENGC | I2C_CR1_NOSTRETCH), (hi2c->Init.GeneralCallMode | hi2c->Init.NoStretchMode));
00534 
00535   /*---------------------------- I2Cx OAR1 Configuration ---------------------*/
00536   /* Configure I2Cx: Own Address1 and addressing mode */
00537   MODIFY_REG(hi2c->Instance->OAR1, (I2C_OAR1_ADDMODE | I2C_OAR1_ADD8_9 | I2C_OAR1_ADD1_7 | I2C_OAR1_ADD0), (hi2c->Init.AddressingMode | hi2c->Init.OwnAddress1));
00538 
00539   /*---------------------------- I2Cx OAR2 Configuration ---------------------*/
00540   /* Configure I2Cx: Dual mode and Own Address2 */
00541   MODIFY_REG(hi2c->Instance->OAR2, (I2C_OAR2_ENDUAL | I2C_OAR2_ADD2), (hi2c->Init.DualAddressMode | hi2c->Init.OwnAddress2));
00542 
00543   /* Enable the selected I2C peripheral */
00544   __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
00545 
00546   hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
00547   hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
00548   hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_NONE;
00549   hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
00550 
00551   return HAL_OK;
00552 }
00553 
00554 /**
00555   * @brief  DeInitialize the I2C peripheral.
00556   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
00557   *         the configuration information for the specified I2C.
00558   * @retval HAL status
00559   */
00560 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_DeInit(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
00561 {
00562   /* Check the I2C handle allocation */
00563   if (hi2c == NULL)
00564   {
00565     return HAL_ERROR;
00566   }
00567 
00568   /* Check the parameters */
00569   assert_param(IS_I2C_ALL_INSTANCE(hi2c->Instance));
00570 
00571   hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY;
00572 
00573   /* Disable the I2C Peripheral Clock */
00574   __HAL_I2C_DISABLE(hi2c);
00575 
00576 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
00577   if (hi2c->MspDeInitCallback == NULL)
00578   {
00579     hi2c->MspDeInitCallback = HAL_I2C_MspDeInit; /* Legacy weak MspDeInit  */
00580   }
00581 
00582   /* DeInit the low level hardware: GPIO, CLOCK, NVIC */
00583   hi2c->MspDeInitCallback(hi2c);
00584 #else
00585   /* DeInit the low level hardware: GPIO, CLOCK, NVIC */
00586   HAL_I2C_MspDeInit(hi2c);
00587 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
00588 
00589   hi2c->ErrorCode     = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
00590   hi2c->State         = HAL_I2C_STATE_RESET;
00591   hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_NONE;
00592   hi2c->Mode          = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
00593 
00594   /* Release Lock */
00595   __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
00596 
00597   return HAL_OK;
00598 }

00605   */
00606 __weak void HAL_I2C_MspInit(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
00607 {
00608   /* Prevent unused argument(s) compilation warning */
00609   UNUSED(hi2c);
00610

00612             the HAL_I2C_MspInit could be implemented in the user file

00616 /**
00617   * @brief  DeInitialize the I2C MSP.
00618   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
00619   *         the configuration information for the specified I2C.
00620   * @retval None
00621   */
00622 __weak void HAL_I2C_MspDeInit(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
00623 {
00624   /* Prevent unused argument(s) compilation warning */
00625   UNUSED(hi2c);
00626 
00627   /* NOTE : This function should not be modified, when the callback is needed,
00628             the HAL_I2C_MspDeInit could be implemented in the user file
00629    */
00630 }
00631 
00632 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
00633 /**
00634   * @brief  Register a User I2C Callback
00635   *         To be used instead of the weak predefined callback
00636   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
00637   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
00638   * @param  CallbackID ID of the callback to be registered
00639   *         This parameter can be one of the following values:
00640   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_MASTER_TX_COMPLETE_CB_ID Master Tx Transfer completed callback ID
00641   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_MASTER_RX_COMPLETE_CB_ID Master Rx Transfer completed callback ID
00642   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_SLAVE_TX_COMPLETE_CB_ID Slave Tx Transfer completed callback ID
00643   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_SLAVE_RX_COMPLETE_CB_ID Slave Rx Transfer completed callback ID
00644   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_LISTEN_COMPLETE_CB_ID Listen Complete callback ID
00645   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_MEM_TX_COMPLETE_CB_ID Memory Tx Transfer callback ID
00646   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_MEM_RX_COMPLETE_CB_ID Memory Rx Transfer completed callback ID
00647   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_ERROR_CB_ID Error callback ID
00648   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_ABORT_CB_ID Abort callback ID
00649   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_MSPINIT_CB_ID MspInit callback ID
00650   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_MSPDEINIT_CB_ID MspDeInit callback ID
00651   * @param  pCallback pointer to the Callback function
00652   * @retval HAL status
00653   */
00654 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_RegisterCallback(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, HAL_I2C_CallbackIDTypeDef CallbackID, pI2C_CallbackTypeDef pCallback)
00655 {
00656   HAL_StatusTypeDef status = HAL_OK;
00657 
00658   if (pCallback == NULL)
00659   {
00660     /* Update the error code */
00661     hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_INVALID_CALLBACK;
00662 
00663     return HAL_ERROR;
00664   }
00665   /* Process locked */
00666   __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
00667 
00668   if (HAL_I2C_STATE_READY == hi2c->State)
00669   {
00670     switch (CallbackID)
00671     {
00672       case HAL_I2C_MASTER_TX_COMPLETE_CB_ID :
00673         hi2c->MasterTxCpltCallback = pCallback;
00674         break;
00675 
00676       case HAL_I2C_MASTER_RX_COMPLETE_CB_ID :
00677         hi2c->MasterRxCpltCallback = pCallback;
00678         break;
00679 
00680       case HAL_I2C_SLAVE_TX_COMPLETE_CB_ID :
00681         hi2c->SlaveTxCpltCallback = pCallback;
00682         break;
00683 
00684       case HAL_I2C_SLAVE_RX_COMPLETE_CB_ID :
00685         hi2c->SlaveRxCpltCallback = pCallback;
00686         break;
00687 
00688       case HAL_I2C_LISTEN_COMPLETE_CB_ID :
00689         hi2c->ListenCpltCallback = pCallback;
00690         break;
00691 
00692       case HAL_I2C_MEM_TX_COMPLETE_CB_ID :
00693         hi2c->MemTxCpltCallback = pCallback;
00694         break;
00695 
00696       case HAL_I2C_MEM_RX_COMPLETE_CB_ID :
00697         hi2c->MemRxCpltCallback = pCallback;
00698         break;
00699 
00700       case HAL_I2C_ERROR_CB_ID :
00701         hi2c->ErrorCallback = pCallback;
00702         break;
00703 
00704       case HAL_I2C_ABORT_CB_ID :
00705         hi2c->AbortCpltCallback = pCallback;
00706         break;
00707 
00708       case HAL_I2C_MSPINIT_CB_ID :
00709         hi2c->MspInitCallback = pCallback;
00710         break;
00711 
00712       case HAL_I2C_MSPDEINIT_CB_ID :
00713         hi2c->MspDeInitCallback = pCallback;
00714         break;
00715 
00716       default :
00717         /* Update the error code */
00718         hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_INVALID_CALLBACK;
00719 
00720         /* Return error status */
00721         status =  HAL_ERROR;
00722         break;
00723     }
00724   }
00725   else if (HAL_I2C_STATE_RESET == hi2c->State)
00726   {
00727     switch (CallbackID)
00728     {
00729       case HAL_I2C_MSPINIT_CB_ID :
00730         hi2c->MspInitCallback = pCallback;
00731         break;
00732 
00733       case HAL_I2C_MSPDEINIT_CB_ID :
00734         hi2c->MspDeInitCallback = pCallback;
00735         break;
00736 
00737       default :
00738         /* Update the error code */
00739         hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_INVALID_CALLBACK;
00740 
00741         /* Return error status */
00742         status =  HAL_ERROR;
00743         break;
00744     }
00745   }
00746   else
00747   {
00748     /* Update the error code */
00749     hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_INVALID_CALLBACK;
00750 
00751     /* Return error status */
00752     status =  HAL_ERROR;
00753   }
00754 
00755   /* Release Lock */
00756   __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
00757   return status;
00758 }
00759 
00760 /**
00761   * @brief  Unregister an I2C Callback
00762   *         I2C callback is redirected to the weak predefined callback
00763   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
00764   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
00765   * @param  CallbackID ID of the callback to be unregistered
00766   *         This parameter can be one of the following values:
00767   *         This parameter can be one of the following values:
00768   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_MASTER_TX_COMPLETE_CB_ID Master Tx Transfer completed callback ID
00769   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_MASTER_RX_COMPLETE_CB_ID Master Rx Transfer completed callback ID
00770   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_SLAVE_TX_COMPLETE_CB_ID Slave Tx Transfer completed callback ID
00771   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_SLAVE_RX_COMPLETE_CB_ID Slave Rx Transfer completed callback ID
00772   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_LISTEN_COMPLETE_CB_ID Listen Complete callback ID
00773   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_MEM_TX_COMPLETE_CB_ID Memory Tx Transfer callback ID
00774   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_MEM_RX_COMPLETE_CB_ID Memory Rx Transfer completed callback ID
00775   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_ERROR_CB_ID Error callback ID
00776   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_ABORT_CB_ID Abort callback ID
00777   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_MSPINIT_CB_ID MspInit callback ID
00778   *          @arg @ref HAL_I2C_MSPDEINIT_CB_ID MspDeInit callback ID
00779   * @retval HAL status
00780   */
00781 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_UnRegisterCallback(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, HAL_I2C_CallbackIDTypeDef CallbackID)
00782 {
00783   HAL_StatusTypeDef status = HAL_OK;
00784 
00785   /* Process locked */
00786   __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
00787 
00788   if (HAL_I2C_STATE_READY == hi2c->State)
00789   {
00790     switch (CallbackID)
00791     {
00792       case HAL_I2C_MASTER_TX_COMPLETE_CB_ID :
00793         hi2c->MasterTxCpltCallback = HAL_I2C_MasterTxCpltCallback; /* Legacy weak MasterTxCpltCallback */
00794         break;
00795 
00796       case HAL_I2C_MASTER_RX_COMPLETE_CB_ID :
00797         hi2c->MasterRxCpltCallback = HAL_I2C_MasterRxCpltCallback; /* Legacy weak MasterRxCpltCallback */
00798         break;
00799 
00800       case HAL_I2C_SLAVE_TX_COMPLETE_CB_ID :
00801         hi2c->SlaveTxCpltCallback = HAL_I2C_SlaveTxCpltCallback;   /* Legacy weak SlaveTxCpltCallback  */
00802         break;
00803 
00804       case HAL_I2C_SLAVE_RX_COMPLETE_CB_ID :
00805         hi2c->SlaveRxCpltCallback = HAL_I2C_SlaveRxCpltCallback;   /* Legacy weak SlaveRxCpltCallback  */
00806         break;
00807 
00808       case HAL_I2C_LISTEN_COMPLETE_CB_ID :
00809         hi2c->ListenCpltCallback = HAL_I2C_ListenCpltCallback;     /* Legacy weak ListenCpltCallback   */
00810         break;
00811 
00812       case HAL_I2C_MEM_TX_COMPLETE_CB_ID :
00813         hi2c->MemTxCpltCallback = HAL_I2C_MemTxCpltCallback;       /* Legacy weak MemTxCpltCallback    */
00814         break;
00815 
00816       case HAL_I2C_MEM_RX_COMPLETE_CB_ID :
00817         hi2c->MemRxCpltCallback = HAL_I2C_MemRxCpltCallback;       /* Legacy weak MemRxCpltCallback    */
00818         break;
00819 
00820       case HAL_I2C_ERROR_CB_ID :
00821         hi2c->ErrorCallback = HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback;               /* Legacy weak ErrorCallback        */
00822         break;
00823 
00824       case HAL_I2C_ABORT_CB_ID :
00825         hi2c->AbortCpltCallback = HAL_I2C_AbortCpltCallback;       /* Legacy weak AbortCpltCallback    */
00826         break;
00827 
00828       case HAL_I2C_MSPINIT_CB_ID :
00829         hi2c->MspInitCallback = HAL_I2C_MspInit;                   /* Legacy weak MspInit              */
00830         break;
00831 
00832       case HAL_I2C_MSPDEINIT_CB_ID :
00833         hi2c->MspDeInitCallback = HAL_I2C_MspDeInit;               /* Legacy weak MspDeInit            */
00834         break;
00835 
00836       default :
00837         /* Update the error code */
00838         hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_INVALID_CALLBACK;
00839 
00840         /* Return error status */
00841         status =  HAL_ERROR;
00842         break;
00843     }
00844   }
00845   else if (HAL_I2C_STATE_RESET == hi2c->State)
00846   {
00847     switch (CallbackID)
00848     {
00849       case HAL_I2C_MSPINIT_CB_ID :
00850         hi2c->MspInitCallback = HAL_I2C_MspInit;                   /* Legacy weak MspInit              */
00851         break;
00852 
00853       case HAL_I2C_MSPDEINIT_CB_ID :
00854         hi2c->MspDeInitCallback = HAL_I2C_MspDeInit;               /* Legacy weak MspDeInit            */
00855         break;
00856 
00857       default :
00858         /* Update the error code */
00859         hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_INVALID_CALLBACK;
00860 
00861         /* Return error status */
00862         status =  HAL_ERROR;
00863         break;
00864     }
00865   }
00866   else
00867   {
00868     /* Update the error code */
00869     hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_INVALID_CALLBACK;
00870 
00871     /* Return error status */
00872     status =  HAL_ERROR;
00873   }
00874 
00875   /* Release Lock */
00876   __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
00877   return status;
00878 }

00880 /**
00881   * @brief  Register the Slave Address Match I2C Callback
00882   *         To be used instead of the weak HAL_I2C_AddrCallback() predefined callback
00883   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
00884   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
00885   * @param  pCallback pointer to the Address Match Callback function
00886   * @retval HAL status
00887   */
00888 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_RegisterAddrCallback(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, pI2C_AddrCallbackTypeDef pCallback)
00889 {
00890   HAL_StatusTypeDef status = HAL_OK;
00891 
00892   if (pCallback == NULL)
00893   {
00894     /* Update the error code */
00895     hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_INVALID_CALLBACK;
00896 
00897     return HAL_ERROR;
00898   }
00899   /* Process locked */
00900   __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
00901 
00902   if (HAL_I2C_STATE_READY == hi2c->State)
00903   {
00904     hi2c->AddrCallback = pCallback;
00905   }
00906   else
00907   {
00908     /* Update the error code */
00909     hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_INVALID_CALLBACK;
00910 
00911     /* Return error status */
00912     status =  HAL_ERROR;
00913   }
00914 
00915   /* Release Lock */
00916   __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
00917   return status;
00918 }
00919 
00920 /**
00921   * @brief  UnRegister the Slave Address Match I2C Callback
00922   *         Info Ready I2C Callback is redirected to the weak HAL_I2C_AddrCallback() predefined callback
00923   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
00924   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
00925   * @retval HAL status
00926   */
00927 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_UnRegisterAddrCallback(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
00928 {
00929   HAL_StatusTypeDef status = HAL_OK;
00930 
00931   /* Process locked */
00932   __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
00933 
00934   if (HAL_I2C_STATE_READY == hi2c->State)
00935   {
00936     hi2c->AddrCallback = HAL_I2C_AddrCallback; /* Legacy weak AddrCallback  */
00937   }
00938   else
00939   {
00940     /* Update the error code */
00941     hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_INVALID_CALLBACK;
00942 
00943     /* Return error status */
00944     status =  HAL_ERROR;
00945   }
00946 
00947   /* Release Lock */
00948   __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
00949   return status;
00950 }
00951 
00952 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
00953 
00954 /**
00955   * @}
00956   */
00957 
00958 /** @defgroup I2C_Exported_Functions_Group2 Input and Output operation functions
00959  *  @brief   Data transfers functions
00960  *
00961 @verbatim
00962  ===============================================================================
00963                       ##### IO operation functions #####
00964  ===============================================================================
00965     [..]
00966     This subsection provides a set of functions allowing to manage the I2C data
00967     transfers.
00968 
00969     (#) There are two modes of transfer:
00970        (++) Blocking mode : The communication is performed in the polling mode.
00971             The status of all data processing is returned by the same function
00972             after finishing transfer.
00973        (++) No-Blocking mode : The communication is performed using Interrupts
00974             or DMA. These functions return the status of the transfer startup.
00975             The end of the data processing will be indicated through the
00976             dedicated I2C IRQ when using Interrupt mode or the DMA IRQ when
00977             using DMA mode.
00978 
00979     (#) Blocking mode functions are :
00980         (++) HAL_I2C_Master_Transmit()
00981         (++) HAL_I2C_Master_Receive()
00982         (++) HAL_I2C_Slave_Transmit()
00983         (++) HAL_I2C_Slave_Receive()
00984         (++) HAL_I2C_Mem_Write()
00985         (++) HAL_I2C_Mem_Read()
00986         (++) HAL_I2C_IsDeviceReady()
00987 
00988     (#) No-Blocking mode functions with Interrupt are :
00989         (++) HAL_I2C_Master_Transmit_IT()
00990         (++) HAL_I2C_Master_Receive_IT()
00991         (++) HAL_I2C_Slave_Transmit_IT()
00992         (++) HAL_I2C_Slave_Receive_IT()
00993         (++) HAL_I2C_Mem_Write_IT()
00994         (++) HAL_I2C_Mem_Read_IT()
00995         (++) HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Transmit_IT()
00996         (++) HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Receive_IT()
00997         (++) HAL_I2C_Slave_Seq_Transmit_IT()
00998         (++) HAL_I2C_Slave_Seq_Receive_IT()
00999         (++) HAL_I2C_EnableListen_IT()
01000         (++) HAL_I2C_DisableListen_IT()
01001         (++) HAL_I2C_Master_Abort_IT()
01002 
01003     (#) No-Blocking mode functions with DMA are :
01004         (++) HAL_I2C_Master_Transmit_DMA()
01005         (++) HAL_I2C_Master_Receive_DMA()
01006         (++) HAL_I2C_Slave_Transmit_DMA()
01007         (++) HAL_I2C_Slave_Receive_DMA()
01008         (++) HAL_I2C_Mem_Write_DMA()
01009         (++) HAL_I2C_Mem_Read_DMA()
01010         (++) HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Transmit_DMA()
01011         (++) HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Receive_DMA()
01012         (++) HAL_I2C_Slave_Seq_Transmit_DMA()
01013         (++) HAL_I2C_Slave_Seq_Receive_DMA()
01014 
01015     (#) A set of Transfer Complete Callbacks are provided in non Blocking mode:
01016         (++) HAL_I2C_MasterTxCpltCallback()
01017         (++) HAL_I2C_MasterRxCpltCallback()
01018         (++) HAL_I2C_SlaveTxCpltCallback()
01019         (++) HAL_I2C_SlaveRxCpltCallback()
01020         (++) HAL_I2C_MemTxCpltCallback()
01021         (++) HAL_I2C_MemRxCpltCallback()
01022         (++) HAL_I2C_AddrCallback()
01023         (++) HAL_I2C_ListenCpltCallback()
01024         (++) HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback()
01025         (++) HAL_I2C_AbortCpltCallback()
01026 
01027 @endverbatim
01028   * @{
01029   */
01030 
01031 /**
01032   * @brief  Transmits in master mode an amount of data in blocking mode.
01033   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
01034   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
01035   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
01036   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
01037   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
01038   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
01039   * @param  Timeout Timeout duration
01040   * @retval HAL status
01041   */
01042 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Master_Transmit(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size, uint32_t Timeout)
01043 {
01044   /* Init tickstart for timeout management*/
01045   uint32_t tickstart = HAL_GetTick();
01046 
01047   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
01048   {
01049     /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
01050     if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY, SET, I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01051     {
01052       return HAL_BUSY;
01053     }
01054 
01055     /* Process Locked */
01056     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
01057 
01058     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
01059     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
01060     {
01061       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
01062       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
01063     }
01064 
01065     /* Disable Pos */
01066     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
01067 
01068     hi2c->State       = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX;
01069     hi2c->Mode        = HAL_I2C_MODE_MASTER;
01070     hi2c->ErrorCode   = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
01071 
01072     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
01073     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
01074     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
01075     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
01076     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
01077 
01078     /* Send Slave Address */
01079     if (I2C_MasterRequestWrite(hi2c, DevAddress, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01080     {
01081       return HAL_ERROR;
01082     }
01083 
01084     /* Clear ADDR flag */
01085     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
01086 
01087     while (hi2c->XferSize > 0U)
01088     {
01089       /* Wait until TXE flag is set */
01090       if (I2C_WaitOnTXEFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01091       {
01092         if (hi2c->ErrorCode == HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF)
01093         {
01094           /* Generate Stop */
01095           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
01096         }
01097         return HAL_ERROR;
01098       }
01099 
01100       /* Write data to DR */
01101       hi2c->Instance->DR = *hi2c->pBuffPtr;
01102 
01103       /* Increment Buffer pointer */
01104       hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
01105 
01106       /* Update counter */
01107       hi2c->XferCount--;
01108       hi2c->XferSize--;
01109 
01110       if ((__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BTF) == SET) && (hi2c->XferSize != 0U))
01111       {
01112         /* Write data to DR */
01113         hi2c->Instance->DR = *hi2c->pBuffPtr;
01114 
01115         /* Increment Buffer pointer */
01116         hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
01117 
01118         /* Update counter */
01119         hi2c->XferCount--;
01120         hi2c->XferSize--;
01121       }
01122 
01123       /* Wait until BTF flag is set */
01124       if (I2C_WaitOnBTFFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01125       {
01126         if (hi2c->ErrorCode == HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF)
01127         {
01128           /* Generate Stop */
01129           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
01130         }
01131         return HAL_ERROR;
01132       }
01133     }
01134 
01135     /* Generate Stop */
01136     SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
01137 
01138     hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
01139     hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
01140 
01141     /* Process Unlocked */
01142     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
01143 
01144     return HAL_OK;
01145   }
01146   else
01147   {
01148     return HAL_BUSY;
01149   }
01150 }
01151 
01152 /**
01153   * @brief  Receives in master mode an amount of data in blocking mode.
01154   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
01155   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
01156   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
01157   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
01158   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
01159   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
01160   * @param  Timeout Timeout duration
01161   * @retval HAL status
01162   */
01163 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Master_Receive(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size, uint32_t Timeout)
01164 {
01165   /* Init tickstart for timeout management*/
01166   uint32_t tickstart = HAL_GetTick();
01167 
01168   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
01169   {
01170     /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
01171     if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY, SET, I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01172     {
01173       return HAL_BUSY;
01174     }
01175 
01176     /* Process Locked */
01177     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
01178 
01179     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
01180     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
01181     {
01182       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
01183       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
01184     }
01185 
01186     /* Disable Pos */
01187     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
01188 
01189     hi2c->State       = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX;
01190     hi2c->Mode        = HAL_I2C_MODE_MASTER;
01191     hi2c->ErrorCode   = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
01192 
01193     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
01194     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
01195     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
01196     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
01197     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
01198 
01199     /* Send Slave Address */
01200     if (I2C_MasterRequestRead(hi2c, DevAddress, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01201     {
01202       return HAL_ERROR;
01203     }
01204 
01205     if (hi2c->XferSize == 0U)
01206     {
01207       /* Clear ADDR flag */
01208       __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
01209 
01210       /* Generate Stop */
01211       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
01212     }
01213     else if (hi2c->XferSize == 1U)
01214     {
01215       /* Disable Acknowledge */
01216       CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
01217 
01218       /* Disable all active IRQs around ADDR clearing and STOP programming because the EV6_3
01219       software sequence must complete before the current byte end of transfer */
01220       __disable_irq();
01221 
01222       /* Clear ADDR flag */
01223       __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
01224 
01225       /* Generate Stop */
01226       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
01227 
01228       /* Re-enable IRQs */
01229       __enable_irq();
01230     }
01231     else if (hi2c->XferSize == 2U)
01232     {
01233       /* Enable Pos */
01234       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
01235 
01236       /* Disable all active IRQs around ADDR clearing and STOP programming because the EV6_3
01237       software sequence must complete before the current byte end of transfer */
01238       __disable_irq();
01239 
01240       /* Clear ADDR flag */
01241       __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
01242 
01243       /* Disable Acknowledge */
01244       CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
01245 
01246       /* Re-enable IRQs */
01247       __enable_irq();
01248     }
01249     else
01250     {
01251       /* Enable Acknowledge */
01252       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
01253 
01254       /* Clear ADDR flag */
01255       __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
01256     }
01257 
01258     while (hi2c->XferSize > 0U)
01259     {
01260       if (hi2c->XferSize <= 3U)
01261       {
01262         /* One byte */
01263         if (hi2c->XferSize == 1U)
01264         {
01265           /* Wait until RXNE flag is set */
01266           if (I2C_WaitOnRXNEFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01267           {
01268             return HAL_ERROR;
01269           }
01270 
01271           /* Read data from DR */
01272           *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
01273 
01274           /* Increment Buffer pointer */
01275           hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
01276 
01277           /* Update counter */
01278           hi2c->XferSize--;
01279           hi2c->XferCount--;
01280         }
01281         /* Two bytes */
01282         else if (hi2c->XferSize == 2U)
01283         {
01284           /* Wait until BTF flag is set */
01285           if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BTF, RESET, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01286           {
01287             return HAL_ERROR;
01288           }
01289 
01290           /* Disable all active IRQs around ADDR clearing and STOP programming because the EV6_3
01291              software sequence must complete before the current byte end of transfer */
01292           __disable_irq();
01293 
01294           /* Generate Stop */
01295           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
01296 
01297           /* Read data from DR */
01298           *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
01299 
01300           /* Increment Buffer pointer */
01301           hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
01302 
01303           /* Update counter */
01304           hi2c->XferSize--;
01305           hi2c->XferCount--;
01306 
01307           /* Re-enable IRQs */
01308           __enable_irq();
01309 
01310           /* Read data from DR */
01311           *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
01312 
01313           /* Increment Buffer pointer */
01314           hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
01315 
01316           /* Update counter */
01317           hi2c->XferSize--;
01318           hi2c->XferCount--;
01319         }
01320         /* 3 Last bytes */
01321         else
01322         {
01323           /* Wait until BTF flag is set */
01324           if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BTF, RESET, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01325           {
01326             return HAL_ERROR;
01327           }
01328 
01329           /* Disable Acknowledge */
01330           CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
01331 
01332           /* Disable all active IRQs around ADDR clearing and STOP programming because the EV6_3
01333              software sequence must complete before the current byte end of transfer */
01334           __disable_irq();
01335 
01336           /* Read data from DR */
01337           *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
01338 
01339           /* Increment Buffer pointer */
01340           hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
01341 
01342           /* Update counter */
01343           hi2c->XferSize--;
01344           hi2c->XferCount--;
01345 
01346           /* Wait until BTF flag is set */
01347           if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BTF, RESET, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01348           {
01349             return HAL_ERROR;
01350           }
01351 
01352           /* Generate Stop */
01353           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
01354 
01355           /* Read data from DR */
01356           *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
01357 
01358           /* Increment Buffer pointer */
01359           hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
01360 
01361           /* Update counter */
01362           hi2c->XferSize--;
01363           hi2c->XferCount--;
01364 
01365           /* Re-enable IRQs */
01366           __enable_irq();
01367 
01368           /* Read data from DR */
01369           *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
01370 
01371           /* Increment Buffer pointer */
01372           hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
01373 
01374           /* Update counter */
01375           hi2c->XferSize--;
01376           hi2c->XferCount--;
01377         }
01378       }
01379       else
01380       {
01381         /* Wait until RXNE flag is set */
01382         if (I2C_WaitOnRXNEFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01383         {
01384           return HAL_ERROR;
01385         }
01386 
01387         /* Read data from DR */
01388         *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
01389 
01390         /* Increment Buffer pointer */
01391         hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
01392 
01393         /* Update counter */
01394         hi2c->XferSize--;
01395         hi2c->XferCount--;
01396 
01397         if (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BTF) == SET)
01398         {
01399           /* Read data from DR */
01400           *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
01401 
01402           /* Increment Buffer pointer */
01403           hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
01404 
01405           /* Update counter */
01406           hi2c->XferSize--;
01407           hi2c->XferCount--;
01408         }
01409       }
01410     }
01411 
01412     hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
01413     hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
01414 
01415     /* Process Unlocked */
01416     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
01417 
01418     return HAL_OK;
01419   }
01420   else
01421   {
01422     return HAL_BUSY;
01423   }
01424 }
01425 
01426 /**
01427   * @brief  Transmits in slave mode an amount of data in blocking mode.
01428   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
01429   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
01430   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
01431   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
01432   * @param  Timeout Timeout duration
01433   * @retval HAL status
01434   */
01435 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Slave_Transmit(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size, uint32_t Timeout)
01436 {
01437   /* Init tickstart for timeout management*/
01438   uint32_t tickstart = HAL_GetTick();
01439 
01440   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
01441   {
01442     if ((pData == NULL) || (Size == 0U))
01443     {
01444       return  HAL_ERROR;
01445     }
01446 
01447     /* Process Locked */
01448     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
01449 
01450     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
01451     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
01452     {
01453       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
01454       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
01455     }
01456 
01457     /* Disable Pos */
01458     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
01459 
01460     hi2c->State       = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX;
01461     hi2c->Mode        = HAL_I2C_MODE_SLAVE;
01462     hi2c->ErrorCode   = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
01463 
01464     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
01465     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
01466     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
01467     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
01468     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
01469 
01470     /* Enable Address Acknowledge */
01471     SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
01472 
01473     /* Wait until ADDR flag is set */
01474     if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_ADDR, RESET, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01475     {
01476       return HAL_ERROR;
01477     }
01478 
01479     /* Clear ADDR flag */
01480     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
01481 
01482     /* If 10bit addressing mode is selected */
01483     if (hi2c->Init.AddressingMode == I2C_ADDRESSINGMODE_10BIT)
01484     {
01485       /* Wait until ADDR flag is set */
01486       if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_ADDR, RESET, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01487       {
01488         return HAL_ERROR;
01489       }
01490 
01491       /* Clear ADDR flag */
01492       __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
01493     }
01494 
01495     while (hi2c->XferSize > 0U)
01496     {
01497       /* Wait until TXE flag is set */
01498       if (I2C_WaitOnTXEFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01499       {
01500         /* Disable Address Acknowledge */
01501         CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
01502 
01503         return HAL_ERROR;
01504       }
01505 
01506       /* Write data to DR */
01507       hi2c->Instance->DR = *hi2c->pBuffPtr;
01508 
01509       /* Increment Buffer pointer */
01510       hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
01511 
01512       /* Update counter */
01513       hi2c->XferCount--;
01514       hi2c->XferSize--;
01515 
01516       if ((__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BTF) == SET) && (hi2c->XferSize != 0U))
01517       {
01518         /* Write data to DR */
01519         hi2c->Instance->DR = *hi2c->pBuffPtr;
01520 
01521         /* Increment Buffer pointer */
01522         hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
01523 
01524         /* Update counter */
01525         hi2c->XferCount--;
01526         hi2c->XferSize--;
01527       }
01528     }
01529 
01530     /* Wait until AF flag is set */
01531     if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_AF, RESET, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01532     {
01533       return HAL_ERROR;
01534     }
01535 
01536     /* Clear AF flag */
01537     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_AF);
01538 
01539     /* Disable Address Acknowledge */
01540     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
01541 
01542     hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
01543     hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
01544 
01545     /* Process Unlocked */
01546     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
01547 
01548     return HAL_OK;
01549   }
01550   else
01551   {
01552     return HAL_BUSY;
01553   }
01554 }
01555 
01556 /**
01557   * @brief  Receive in slave mode an amount of data in blocking mode
01558   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
01559   *         the configuration information for the specified I2C.
01560   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
01561   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
01562   * @param  Timeout Timeout duration
01563   * @retval HAL status
01564   */
01565 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Slave_Receive(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size, uint32_t Timeout)
01566 {
01567   /* Init tickstart for timeout management*/
01568   uint32_t tickstart = HAL_GetTick();
01569 
01570   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
01571   {
01572     if ((pData == NULL) || (Size == (uint16_t)0))
01573     {
01574       return HAL_ERROR;
01575     }
01576 
01577     /* Process Locked */
01578     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
01579 
01580     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
01581     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
01582     {
01583       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
01584       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
01585     }
01586 
01587     /* Disable Pos */
01588     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
01589 
01590     hi2c->State       = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX;
01591     hi2c->Mode        = HAL_I2C_MODE_SLAVE;
01592     hi2c->ErrorCode   = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
01593 
01594     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
01595     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
01596     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
01597     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
01598     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
01599 
01600     /* Enable Address Acknowledge */
01601     SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
01602 
01603     /* Wait until ADDR flag is set */
01604     if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_ADDR, RESET, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01605     {
01606       return HAL_ERROR;
01607     }
01608 
01609     /* Clear ADDR flag */
01610     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
01611 
01612     while (hi2c->XferSize > 0U)
01613     {
01614       /* Wait until RXNE flag is set */
01615       if (I2C_WaitOnRXNEFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01616       {
01617         /* Disable Address Acknowledge */
01618         CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
01619 
01620         return HAL_ERROR;
01621       }
01622 
01623       /* Read data from DR */
01624       *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
01625 
01626       /* Increment Buffer pointer */
01627       hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
01628 
01629       /* Update counter */
01630       hi2c->XferSize--;
01631       hi2c->XferCount--;
01632 
01633       if ((__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BTF) == SET) && (hi2c->XferSize != 0U))
01634       {
01635         /* Read data from DR */
01636         *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
01637 
01638         /* Increment Buffer pointer */
01639         hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
01640 
01641         /* Update counter */
01642         hi2c->XferSize--;
01643         hi2c->XferCount--;
01644       }
01645     }
01646 
01647     /* Wait until STOP flag is set */
01648     if (I2C_WaitOnSTOPFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
01649     {
01650       /* Disable Address Acknowledge */
01651       CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
01652 
01653       return HAL_ERROR;
01654     }
01655 
01656     /* Clear STOP flag */
01657     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_STOPFLAG(hi2c);
01658 
01659     /* Disable Address Acknowledge */
01660     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
01661 
01662     hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
01663     hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
01664 
01665     /* Process Unlocked */
01666     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
01667 
01668     return HAL_OK;
01669   }
01670   else
01671   {
01672     return HAL_BUSY;
01673   }
01674 }
01675 
01676 /**
01677   * @brief  Transmit in master mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode with Interrupt
01678   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
01679   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
01680   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
01681   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
01682   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
01683   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
01684   * @retval HAL status
01685   */
01686 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Master_Transmit_IT(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size)
01687 {
01688   __IO uint32_t count = 0U;
01689 
01690   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
01691   {
01692     /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
01693     count = I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG * (SystemCoreClock / 25U / 1000U);
01694     do
01695     {
01696       count--;
01697       if (count == 0U)
01698       {
01699         hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
01700         hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
01701         hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
01702         hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_TIMEOUT;
01703 
01704         /* Process Unlocked */
01705         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
01706 
01707         return HAL_ERROR;
01708       }
01709     }
01710     while (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY) != RESET);
01711 
01712     /* Process Locked */
01713     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
01714 
01715     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
01716     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
01717     {
01718       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
01719       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
01720     }
01721 
01722     /* Disable Pos */
01723     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
01724 
01725     hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX;
01726     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_MASTER;
01727     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
01728 
01729     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
01730     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
01731     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
01732     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
01733     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
01734     hi2c->Devaddress  = DevAddress;
01735 
01736     /* Generate Start */
01737     SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
01738 
01739     /* Process Unlocked */
01740     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
01741 
01742     /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
01743               to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
01744               process unlock */
01745     /* Enable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
01746     __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
01747 
01748     return HAL_OK;
01749   }
01750   else
01751   {
01752     return HAL_BUSY;
01753   }
01754 }
