01964 /**
01965   * @brief  Transmit in master mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode with DMA
01966   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
01967   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
01968   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
01969   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
01970   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
01971   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
01972   * @retval HAL status
01973   */
01974 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Master_Transmit_DMA(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size)
01975 {
01976   __IO uint32_t count = 0U;
01977   HAL_StatusTypeDef dmaxferstatus;
01978 
01979   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
01980   {
01981     /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
01982     count = I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG * (SystemCoreClock / 25U / 1000U);
01983     do
01984     {
01985       count--;
01986       if (count == 0U)
01987       {
01988         hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
01989         hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
01990         hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
01991         hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_TIMEOUT;
01992 
01993         /* Process Unlocked */
01994         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
01995 
01996         return HAL_ERROR;
01997       }
01998     }
01999     while (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY) != RESET);
02000 
02001     /* Process Locked */
02002     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
02003 
02004     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
02005     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
02006     {
02007       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
02008       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
02009     }
02010 
02011     /* Disable Pos */
02012     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
02013 
02014     hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX;
02015     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_MASTER;
02016     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
02017 
02018     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
02019     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
02020     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
02021     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
02022     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
02023     hi2c->Devaddress  = DevAddress;
02024 
02025     if (hi2c->XferSize > 0U)
02026     {
02027       /* Set the I2C DMA transfer complete callback */
02028       hi2c->hdmatx->XferCpltCallback = I2C_DMAXferCplt;
02029 
02030       /* Set the DMA error callback */
02031       hi2c->hdmatx->XferErrorCallback = I2C_DMAError;
02032 
02033       /* Set the unused DMA callbacks to NULL */
02034       hi2c->hdmatx->XferHalfCpltCallback = NULL;
02035       hi2c->hdmatx->XferAbortCallback = NULL;
02036 
02037       /* Enable the DMA channel */
02038       dmaxferstatus = HAL_DMA_Start_IT(hi2c->hdmatx, (uint32_t)hi2c->pBuffPtr, (uint32_t)&hi2c->Instance->DR, hi2c->XferSize);
02039 
02040       if (dmaxferstatus == HAL_OK)
02041       {
02042         /* Enable Acknowledge */
02043         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
02044 
02045         /* Generate Start */
02046         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
02047 
02048         /* Process Unlocked */
02049         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
02050 
02051         /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
02052         to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
02053         process unlock */
02054 
02055         /* Enable EVT and ERR interrupt */
02056         __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_ERR);
02057 
02058         /* Enable DMA Request */
02059         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN);
02060       }
02061       else
02062       {
02063         /* Update I2C state */
02064         hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
02065         hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
02066 
02067         /* Update I2C error code */
02068         hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_DMA;
02069 
02070         /* Process Unlocked */
02071         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
02072 
02073         return HAL_ERROR;
02074       }
02075     }
02076     else
02077     {
02078       /* Enable Acknowledge */
02079       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
02080 
02081       /* Generate Start */
02082       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
02083 
02084       /* Process Unlocked */
02085       __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
02086 
02087       /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
02088       to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
02089       process unlock */
02090 
02091       /* Enable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
02092       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
02093     }
02094 
02095     return HAL_OK;
02096   }
02097   else
02098   {
02099     return HAL_BUSY;
02100   }
02101 }
02102 
02103 /**
02104   * @brief  Receive in master mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode with DMA
02105   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
02106   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
02107   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
02108   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
02109   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
02110   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
02111   * @retval HAL status
02112   */
02113 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Master_Receive_DMA(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size)
02114 {
02115   __IO uint32_t count = 0U;
02116   HAL_StatusTypeDef dmaxferstatus;
02117 
02118   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
02119   {
02120     /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
02121     count = I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG * (SystemCoreClock / 25U / 1000U);
02122     do
02123     {
02124       count--;
02125       if (count == 0U)
02126       {
02127         hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
02128         hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
02129         hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
02130         hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_TIMEOUT;
02131 
02132         /* Process Unlocked */
02133         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
02134 
02135         return HAL_ERROR;
02136       }
02137     }
02138     while (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY) != RESET);
02139 
02140     /* Process Locked */
02141     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
02142 
02143     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
02144     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
02145     {
02146       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
02147       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
02148     }
02149 
02150     /* Disable Pos */
02151     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
02152 
02153     hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX;
02154     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_MASTER;
02155     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
02156 
02157     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
02158     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
02159     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
02160     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
02161     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
02162     hi2c->Devaddress  = DevAddress;
02163 
02164     if (hi2c->XferSize > 0U)
02165     {
02166       /* Set the I2C DMA transfer complete callback */
02167       hi2c->hdmarx->XferCpltCallback = I2C_DMAXferCplt;
02168 
02169       /* Set the DMA error callback */
02170       hi2c->hdmarx->XferErrorCallback = I2C_DMAError;
02171 
02172       /* Set the unused DMA callbacks to NULL */
02173       hi2c->hdmarx->XferHalfCpltCallback = NULL;
02174       hi2c->hdmarx->XferAbortCallback = NULL;
02175 
02176       /* Enable the DMA channel */
02177       dmaxferstatus = HAL_DMA_Start_IT(hi2c->hdmarx, (uint32_t)&hi2c->Instance->DR, (uint32_t)hi2c->pBuffPtr, hi2c->XferSize);
02178 
02179       if (dmaxferstatus == HAL_OK)
02180       {
02181         /* Enable Acknowledge */
02182         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
02183 
02184         /* Generate Start */
02185         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
02186 
02187         /* Process Unlocked */
02188         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
02189 
02190         /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
02191         to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
02192         process unlock */
02193 
02194         /* Enable EVT and ERR interrupt */
02195         __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_ERR);
02196 
02197         /* Enable DMA Request */
02198         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN);
02199       }
02200       else
02201       {
02202         /* Update I2C state */
02203         hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
02204         hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
02205 
02206         /* Update I2C error code */
02207         hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_DMA;
02208 
02209         /* Process Unlocked */
02210         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
02211 
02212         return HAL_ERROR;
02213       }
02214     }
02215     else
02216     {
02217       /* Enable Acknowledge */
02218       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
02219 
02220       /* Generate Start */
02221       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
02222 
02223       /* Process Unlocked */
02224       __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
02225 
02226       /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
02227       to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
02228       process unlock */
02229 
02230       /* Enable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
02231       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
02232     }
02233 
02234     return HAL_OK;
02235   }
02236   else
02237   {
02238     return HAL_BUSY;
02239   }
02240 }
02241 
02242 /**
02243   * @brief  Transmit in slave mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode with DMA
02244   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
02245   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
02246   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
02247   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
02248   * @retval HAL status
02249   */
02250 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Slave_Transmit_DMA(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size)
02251 {
02252   HAL_StatusTypeDef dmaxferstatus;
02253 
02254   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
02255   {
02256     if ((pData == NULL) || (Size == 0U))
02257     {
02258       return  HAL_ERROR;
02259     }
02260 
02261     /* Process Locked */
02262     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
02263 
02264     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
02265     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
02266     {
02267       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
02268       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
02269     }
02270 
02271     /* Disable Pos */
02272     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
02273 
02274     hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX;
02275     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_SLAVE;
02276     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
02277 
02278     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
02279     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
02280     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
02281     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
02282     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
02283 
02284     /* Set the I2C DMA transfer complete callback */
02285     hi2c->hdmatx->XferCpltCallback = I2C_DMAXferCplt;
02286 
02287     /* Set the DMA error callback */
02288     hi2c->hdmatx->XferErrorCallback = I2C_DMAError;
02289 
02290     /* Set the unused DMA callbacks to NULL */
02291     hi2c->hdmatx->XferHalfCpltCallback = NULL;
02292     hi2c->hdmatx->XferAbortCallback = NULL;
02293 
02294     /* Enable the DMA channel */
02295     dmaxferstatus = HAL_DMA_Start_IT(hi2c->hdmatx, (uint32_t)hi2c->pBuffPtr, (uint32_t)&hi2c->Instance->DR, hi2c->XferSize);
02296 
02297     if (dmaxferstatus == HAL_OK)
02298     {
02299       /* Enable Address Acknowledge */
02300       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
02301 
02302       /* Process Unlocked */
02303       __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
02304 
02305       /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
02306       to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
02307       process unlock */
02308       /* Enable EVT and ERR interrupt */
02309       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_ERR);
02310 
02311       /* Enable DMA Request */
02312       hi2c->Instance->CR2 |= I2C_CR2_DMAEN;
02313 
02314       return HAL_OK;
02315     }
02316     else
02317     {
02318       /* Update I2C state */
02319       hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
02320       hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
02321 
02322       /* Update I2C error code */
02323       hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_DMA;
02324 
02325       /* Process Unlocked */
02326       __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
02327 
02328       return HAL_ERROR;
02329     }
02330   }
02331   else
02332   {
02333     return HAL_BUSY;
02334   }
02335 }
02336

02338   * @brief  Receive in slave mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode with DMA

02341   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
02342   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent

02345 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Slave_Receive_DMA(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size)
02346 {

02352     {
02353       return  HAL_ERROR;
02354     }
02355 
02356     /* Process Locked */
02357     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
02358 
02359     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */

02407       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN);
02408 
02409       return HAL_OK;
02410     }
02411     else
02412     {
02413       /* Update I2C state */
02414       hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
02415       hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
02416 
02417       /* Update I2C error code */
02418       hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_DMA;
02419 
02420       /* Process Unlocked */
02421       __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
02422 
02423       return HAL_ERROR;
02424     }
02425   }
02426   else
02427   {
02428     return HAL_BUSY;
02429   }
02430 }
02431 
02432 /**
02433   * @brief  Write an amount of data in blocking mode to a specific memory address
02434   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
02435   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
02436   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
02437   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
02438   * @param  MemAddress Internal memory address
02439   * @param  MemAddSize Size of internal memory address
02440   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
02441   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
02442   * @param  Timeout Timeout duration
02443   * @retval HAL status
02444   */
02445 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Mem_Write(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint16_t MemAddress, uint16_t MemAddSize, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size, uint32_t Timeout)
02446 {
02447   /* Init tickstart for timeout management*/
02448   uint32_t tickstart = HAL_GetTick();
02449 
02450   /* Check the parameters */
02451   assert_param(IS_I2C_MEMADD_SIZE(MemAddSize));
02452 
02453   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
02454   {
02455     /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
02456     if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY, SET, I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
02457     {
02458       return HAL_BUSY;
02459     }
02460 
02461     /* Process Locked */
02462     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
02463 
02464     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
02465     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
02466     {
02467       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
02468       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
02469     }
02470 
02471     /* Disable Pos */
02472     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
02473 
02474     hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX;
02475     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_MEM;
02476     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
02477 
02478     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
02479     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
02480     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
02481     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
02482     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
02483 
02484     /* Send Slave Address and Memory Address */
02485     if (I2C_RequestMemoryWrite(hi2c, DevAddress, MemAddress, MemAddSize, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
02486     {
02487       return HAL_ERROR;
02488     }
02489 
02490     while (hi2c->XferSize > 0U)
02491     {
02492       /* Wait until TXE flag is set */
02493       if (I2C_WaitOnTXEFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
02494       {
02495         if (hi2c->ErrorCode == HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF)
02496         {
02497           /* Generate Stop */
02498           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
02499         }
02500         return HAL_ERROR;
02501       }
02502 
02503       /* Write data to DR */
02504       hi2c->Instance->DR = *hi2c->pBuffPtr;
02505 
02506       /* Increment Buffer pointer */
02507       hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
02508 
02509       /* Update counter */
02510       hi2c->XferSize--;
02511       hi2c->XferCount--;
02512 
02513       if ((__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BTF) == SET) && (hi2c->XferSize != 0U))
02514       {
02515         /* Write data to DR */
02516         hi2c->Instance->DR = *hi2c->pBuffPtr;
02517 
02518         /* Increment Buffer pointer */
02519         hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
02520 
02521         /* Update counter */
02522         hi2c->XferSize--;
02523         hi2c->XferCount--;
02524       }
02525     }
02526 
02527     /* Wait until BTF flag is set */
02528     if (I2C_WaitOnBTFFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
02529     {
02530       if (hi2c->ErrorCode == HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF)
02531       {
02532         /* Generate Stop */
02533         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
02534       }
02535       return HAL_ERROR;
02536     }
02537 
02538     /* Generate Stop */
02539     SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
02540 
02541     hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
02542     hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
02543 
02544     /* Process Unlocked */
02545     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
02546 
02547     return HAL_OK;
02548   }
02549   else
02550   {
02551     return HAL_BUSY;
02552   }
02553 }
02554 
02555 /**
02556   * @brief  Read an amount of data in blocking mode from a specific memory address
02557   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
02558   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
02559   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
02560   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
02561   * @param  MemAddress Internal memory address
02562   * @param  MemAddSize Size of internal memory address
02563   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
02564   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
02565   * @param  Timeout Timeout duration
02566   * @retval HAL status
02567   */
02568 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Mem_Read(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint16_t MemAddress, uint16_t MemAddSize, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size, uint32_t Timeout)
02569 {
02570   /* Init tickstart for timeout management*/
02571   uint32_t tickstart = HAL_GetTick();
02572 
02573   /* Check the parameters */
02574   assert_param(IS_I2C_MEMADD_SIZE(MemAddSize));
02575 
02576   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
02577   {
02578     /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
02579     if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY, SET, I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
02580     {
02581       return HAL_BUSY;
02582     }
02583 
02584     /* Process Locked */
02585     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
02586 
02587     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
02588     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
02589     {
02590       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
02591       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
02592     }
02593 
02594     /* Disable Pos */
02595     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
02596 
02597     hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX;
02598     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_MEM;
02599     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
02600 
02601     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
02602     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
02603     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
02604     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
02605     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
02606 
02607     /* Send Slave Address and Memory Address */
02608     if (I2C_RequestMemoryRead(hi2c, DevAddress, MemAddress, MemAddSize, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
02609     {
02610       return HAL_ERROR;
02611     }
02612 
02613     if (hi2c->XferSize == 0U)
02614     {
02615       /* Clear ADDR flag */
02616       __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
02617 
02618       /* Generate Stop */
02619       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
02620     }
02621     else if (hi2c->XferSize == 1U)
02622     {
02623       /* Disable Acknowledge */
02624       CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
02625 
02626       /* Disable all active IRQs around ADDR clearing and STOP programming because the EV6_3
02627          software sequence must complete before the current byte end of transfer */
02628       __disable_irq();
02629 
02630       /* Clear ADDR flag */
02631       __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
02632 
02633       /* Generate Stop */
02634       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
02635 
02636       /* Re-enable IRQs */
02637       __enable_irq();
02638     }
02639     else if (hi2c->XferSize == 2U)
02640     {
02641       /* Enable Pos */
02642       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
02643 
02644       /* Disable all active IRQs around ADDR clearing and STOP programming because the EV6_3
02645          software sequence must complete before the current byte end of transfer */
02646       __disable_irq();
02647 
02648       /* Clear ADDR flag */
02649       __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
02650 
02651       /* Disable Acknowledge */
02652       CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
02653 
02654       /* Re-enable IRQs */
02655       __enable_irq();
02656     }
02657     else
02658     {
02659       /* Enable Acknowledge */
02660       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
02661       /* Clear ADDR flag */
02662       __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
02663     }
02664 
02665     while (hi2c->XferSize > 0U)
02666     {
02667       if (hi2c->XferSize <= 3U)
02668       {
02669         /* One byte */
02670         if (hi2c->XferSize == 1U)
02671         {
02672           /* Wait until RXNE flag is set */
02673           if (I2C_WaitOnRXNEFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
02674           {
02675             return HAL_ERROR;
02676           }
02677 
02678           /* Read data from DR */
02679           *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
02680 
02681           /* Increment Buffer pointer */
02682           hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
02683 
02684           /* Update counter */
02685           hi2c->XferSize--;
02686           hi2c->XferCount--;
02687         }
02688         /* Two bytes */
02689         else if (hi2c->XferSize == 2U)
02690         {
02691           /* Wait until BTF flag is set */
02692           if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BTF, RESET, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
02693           {
02694             return HAL_ERROR;
02695           }
02696 
02697           /* Disable all active IRQs around ADDR clearing and STOP programming because the EV6_3
02698              software sequence must complete before the current byte end of transfer */
02699           __disable_irq();
02700 
02701           /* Generate Stop */
02702           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
02703 
02704           /* Read data from DR */
02705           *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
02706 
02707           /* Increment Buffer pointer */
02708           hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
02709 
02710           /* Update counter */
02711           hi2c->XferSize--;
02712           hi2c->XferCount--;
02713 
02714           /* Re-enable IRQs */
02715           __enable_irq();
02716 
02717           /* Read data from DR */
02718           *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
02719 
02720           /* Increment Buffer pointer */
02721           hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
02722 
02723           /* Update counter */
02724           hi2c->XferSize--;
02725           hi2c->XferCount--;
02726         }
02727         /* 3 Last bytes */
02728         else
02729         {
02730           /* Wait until BTF flag is set */
02731           if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BTF, RESET, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
02732           {
02733             return HAL_ERROR;
02734           }
02735 
02736           /* Disable Acknowledge */
02737           CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
02738 
02739           /* Disable all active IRQs around ADDR clearing and STOP programming because the EV6_3
02740              software sequence must complete before the current byte end of transfer */
02741           __disable_irq();
02742 
02743           /* Read data from DR */
02744           *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
02745 
02746           /* Increment Buffer pointer */
02747           hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
02748 
02749           /* Update counter */
02750           hi2c->XferSize--;
02751           hi2c->XferCount--;
02752 
02753           /* Wait until BTF flag is set */
02754           if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BTF, RESET, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
02755           {
02756             return HAL_ERROR;
02757           }
02758 
02759           /* Generate Stop */
02760           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
02761 
02762           /* Read data from DR */
02763           *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
02764 
02765           /* Increment Buffer pointer */
02766           hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
02767 
02768           /* Update counter */
02769           hi2c->XferSize--;
02770           hi2c->XferCount--;
02771 
02772           /* Re-enable IRQs */
02773           __enable_irq();
02774 
02775           /* Read data from DR */
02776           *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
02777 
02778           /* Increment Buffer pointer */
02779           hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
02780 
02781           /* Update counter */
02782           hi2c->XferSize--;
02783           hi2c->XferCount--;
02784         }
02785       }
02786       else
02787       {
02788         /* Wait until RXNE flag is set */
02789         if (I2C_WaitOnRXNEFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
02790         {
02791           return HAL_ERROR;
02792         }
02793 
02794         /* Read data from DR */
02795         *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
02796 
02797         /* Increment Buffer pointer */
02798         hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
02799 
02800         /* Update counter */
02801         hi2c->XferSize--;
02802         hi2c->XferCount--;
02803 
02804         if (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BTF) == SET)
02805         {
02806           /* Read data from DR */
02807           *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
02808 
02809           /* Increment Buffer pointer */
02810           hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
02811 
02812           /* Update counter */
02813           hi2c->XferSize--;
02814           hi2c->XferCount--;
02815         }
02816       }
02817     }
02818 
02819     hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
02820     hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
02821 
02822     /* Process Unlocked */
02823     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
02824 
02825     return HAL_OK;
02826   }
02827   else
02828   {
02829     return HAL_BUSY;
02830   }
02831 }
02832 
02833 /**
02834   * @brief  Write an amount of data in non-blocking mode with Interrupt to a specific memory address
02835   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
02836   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
02837   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
02838   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
02839   * @param  MemAddress Internal memory address
02840   * @param  MemAddSize Size of internal memory address
02841   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
02842   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
02843   * @retval HAL status
02844   */
02845 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Mem_Write_IT(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint16_t MemAddress, uint16_t MemAddSize, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size)
02846 {
02847   __IO uint32_t count = 0U;
02848 
02849   /* Check the parameters */
02850   assert_param(IS_I2C_MEMADD_SIZE(MemAddSize));
02851 
02852   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
02853   {
02854     /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
02855     count = I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG * (SystemCoreClock / 25U / 1000U);
02856     do
02857     {
02858       count--;
02859       if (count == 0U)
02860       {
02861         hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
02862         hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
02863         hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
02864         hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_TIMEOUT;
02865 
02866         /* Process Unlocked */
02867         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
02868 
02869         return HAL_ERROR;
02870       }
02871     }
02872     while (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY) != RESET);
02873 
02874     /* Process Locked */
02875     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
02876 
02877     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
02878     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
02879     {
02880       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
02881       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
02882     }
02883 
02884     /* Disable Pos */
02885     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
02886 
02887     hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX;
02888     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_MEM;
02889     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
02890 
02891     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
02892     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
02893     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
02894     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
02895     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
02896     hi2c->Devaddress  = DevAddress;
02897     hi2c->Memaddress  = MemAddress;
02898     hi2c->MemaddSize  = MemAddSize;
02899     hi2c->EventCount  = 0U;
02900 
02901     /* Generate Start */
02902     SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
02903 
02904     /* Process Unlocked */
02905     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
02906 
02907     /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
02908     to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
02909     process unlock */
02910 
02911     /* Enable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
02912     __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
02913 
02914     return HAL_OK;
02915   }
02916   else
02917   {
02918     return HAL_BUSY;
02919   }
02920 }
02921 
02922 /**
02923   * @brief  Read an amount of data in non-blocking mode with Interrupt from a specific memory address
02924   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
02925   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
02926   * @param  DevAddress Target device address
02927   * @param  MemAddress Internal memory address
02928   * @param  MemAddSize Size of internal memory address
02929   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
02930   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
02931   * @retval HAL status
02932   */
02933 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Mem_Read_IT(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint16_t MemAddress, uint16_t MemAddSize, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size)
02934 {
02935   __IO uint32_t count = 0U;
02936 
02937   /* Check the parameters */
02938   assert_param(IS_I2C_MEMADD_SIZE(MemAddSize));
02939 
02940   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
02941   {
02942     /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
02943     count = I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG * (SystemCoreClock / 25U / 1000U);
02944     do
02945     {
02946       count--;
02947       if (count == 0U)
02948       {
02949         hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
02950         hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
02951         hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
02952         hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_TIMEOUT;
02953 
02954         /* Process Unlocked */
02955         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
02956 
02957         return HAL_ERROR;
02958       }
02959     }
02960     while (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY) != RESET);
02961 
02962     /* Process Locked */
02963     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
02964 
02965     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
02966     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
02967     {
02968       /* Enable I2C peripheral */

02973     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
02974 
02975     hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX;
02976     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_MEM;
02977     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
02978 
02979     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
02980     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
02981     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;

02986     hi2c->MemaddSize  = MemAddSize;
02987     hi2c->EventCount  = 0U;
02988 
02989     /* Enable Acknowledge */
02990     SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
02991 
02992     /* Generate Start */
02993     SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
02994 
02995     /* Process Unlocked */
02996     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
02997 
02998     if (hi2c->XferSize > 0U)
02999     {
03000       /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
03001       to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
03002       process unlock */
03003 
03004       /* Enable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
03005       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
03006     }
03007     return HAL_OK;
03008   }
03009   else
03010   {
03011     return HAL_BUSY;
03012   }
03013 }
