03015 /**
03016   * @brief  Write an amount of data in non-blocking mode with DMA to a specific memory address
03017   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
03018   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
03019   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
03020   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
03021   * @param  MemAddress Internal memory address
03022   * @param  MemAddSize Size of internal memory address
03023   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
03024   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
03025   * @retval HAL status
03026   */
03027 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Mem_Write_DMA(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint16_t MemAddress, uint16_t MemAddSize, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size)
03028 {
03029   __IO uint32_t count = 0U;
03030   HAL_StatusTypeDef dmaxferstatus;
03031 
03032   /* Init tickstart for timeout management*/
03033   uint32_t tickstart = HAL_GetTick();
03034 
03035   /* Check the parameters */
03036   assert_param(IS_I2C_MEMADD_SIZE(MemAddSize));
03037 
03038   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
03039   {
03040     /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
03041     count = I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG * (SystemCoreClock / 25U / 1000U);
03042     do
03043     {
03044       count--;
03045       if (count == 0U)
03046       {
03047         hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
03048         hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
03049         hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
03050         hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_TIMEOUT;
03051 
03052         /* Process Unlocked */
03053         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03054 
03055         return HAL_ERROR;
03056       }
03057     }
03058     while (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY) != RESET);
03059 
03060     /* Process Locked */
03061     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
03062 
03063     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
03064     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
03065     {
03066       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
03067       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
03068     }
03069 
03070     /* Disable Pos */
03071     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
03072 
03073     hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX;
03074     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_MEM;
03075     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
03076 
03077     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
03078     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
03079     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
03080     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
03081     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
03082 
03083     if (hi2c->XferSize > 0U)
03084     {
03085       /* Set the I2C DMA transfer complete callback */
03086       hi2c->hdmatx->XferCpltCallback = I2C_DMAXferCplt;
03087 
03088       /* Set the DMA error callback */
03089       hi2c->hdmatx->XferErrorCallback = I2C_DMAError;
03090 
03091       /* Set the unused DMA callbacks to NULL */
03092       hi2c->hdmatx->XferHalfCpltCallback = NULL;
03093       hi2c->hdmatx->XferAbortCallback = NULL;
03094 
03095       /* Enable the DMA channel */
03096       dmaxferstatus = HAL_DMA_Start_IT(hi2c->hdmatx, (uint32_t)hi2c->pBuffPtr, (uint32_t)&hi2c->Instance->DR, hi2c->XferSize);
03097 
03098       if (dmaxferstatus == HAL_OK)
03099       {
03100         /* Send Slave Address and Memory Address */
03101         if (I2C_RequestMemoryWrite(hi2c, DevAddress, MemAddress, MemAddSize, I2C_TIMEOUT_FLAG, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
03102         {
03103           return HAL_ERROR;
03104         }
03105 
03106         /* Clear ADDR flag */
03107         __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
03108 
03109         /* Process Unlocked */
03110         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03111 
03112         /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
03113         to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
03114         process unlock */
03115         /* Enable ERR interrupt */
03116         __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_ERR);
03117 
03118         /* Enable DMA Request */
03119         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN);
03120 
03121         return HAL_OK;
03122       }
03123       else
03124       {
03125         /* Update I2C state */
03126         hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
03127         hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
03128 
03129         /* Update I2C error code */
03130         hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_DMA;
03131 
03132         /* Process Unlocked */
03133         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03134 
03135         return HAL_ERROR;
03136       }
03137     }
03138     else
03139     {
03140       /* Update I2C state */
03141       hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
03142       hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
03143 
03144       /* Update I2C error code */
03145       hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_SIZE;
03146 
03147       /* Process Unlocked */
03148       __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03149 
03150       return HAL_ERROR;
03151     }
03152   }
03153   else
03154   {
03155     return HAL_BUSY;
03156   }
03157 }
03158 
03159 /**
03160   * @brief  Reads an amount of data in non-blocking mode with DMA from a specific memory address.
03161   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
03162   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
03163   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
03164   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
03165   * @param  MemAddress Internal memory address
03166   * @param  MemAddSize Size of internal memory address
03167   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
03168   * @param  Size Amount of data to be read
03169   * @retval HAL status
03170   */
03171 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Mem_Read_DMA(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint16_t MemAddress, uint16_t MemAddSize, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size)
03172 {
03173   /* Init tickstart for timeout management*/
03174   uint32_t tickstart = HAL_GetTick();
03175   __IO uint32_t count = 0U;
03176   HAL_StatusTypeDef dmaxferstatus;
03177 
03178   /* Check the parameters */
03179   assert_param(IS_I2C_MEMADD_SIZE(MemAddSize));
03180 
03181   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
03182   {
03183     /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
03184     count = I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG * (SystemCoreClock / 25U / 1000U);
03185     do
03186     {
03187       count--;
03188       if (count == 0U)
03189       {
03190         hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
03191         hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
03192         hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
03193         hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_TIMEOUT;
03194 
03195         /* Process Unlocked */
03196         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03197 
03198         return HAL_ERROR;
03199       }
03200     }
03201     while (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY) != RESET);
03202 
03203     /* Process Locked */
03204     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
03205 
03206     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
03207     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
03208     {
03209       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
03210       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
03211     }
03212 
03213     /* Disable Pos */
03214     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
03215 
03216     hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX;
03217     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_MEM;
03218     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
03219 
03220     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
03221     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
03222     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
03223     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
03224     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
03225 
03226     if (hi2c->XferSize > 0U)
03227     {
03228       /* Set the I2C DMA transfer complete callback */
03229       hi2c->hdmarx->XferCpltCallback = I2C_DMAXferCplt;
03230 
03231       /* Set the DMA error callback */
03232       hi2c->hdmarx->XferErrorCallback = I2C_DMAError;
03233 
03234       /* Set the unused DMA callbacks to NULL */
03235       hi2c->hdmarx->XferHalfCpltCallback = NULL;
03236       hi2c->hdmarx->XferAbortCallback = NULL;
03237 
03238       /* Enable the DMA channel */
03239       dmaxferstatus = HAL_DMA_Start_IT(hi2c->hdmarx, (uint32_t)&hi2c->Instance->DR, (uint32_t)hi2c->pBuffPtr, hi2c->XferSize);
03240 
03241       if (dmaxferstatus == HAL_OK)
03242       {
03243         /* Send Slave Address and Memory Address */
03244         if (I2C_RequestMemoryRead(hi2c, DevAddress, MemAddress, MemAddSize, I2C_TIMEOUT_FLAG, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
03245         {
03246           return HAL_ERROR;
03247         }
03248 
03249         if (hi2c->XferSize == 1U)
03250         {
03251           /* Disable Acknowledge */
03252           CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
03253         }
03254         else
03255         {
03256           /* Enable Last DMA bit */
03257           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_LAST);
03258         }
03259 
03260         /* Clear ADDR flag */
03261         __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
03262 
03263         /* Process Unlocked */
03264         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03265 
03266         /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
03267         to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
03268         process unlock */
03269         /* Enable ERR interrupt */
03270         __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_ERR);
03271 
03272         /* Enable DMA Request */
03273         hi2c->Instance->CR2 |= I2C_CR2_DMAEN;
03274       }
03275       else
03276       {
03277         /* Update I2C state */
03278         hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
03279         hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
03280 
03281         /* Update I2C error code */
03282         hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_DMA;
03283 
03284         /* Process Unlocked */
03285         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03286 
03287         return HAL_ERROR;
03288       }
03289     }
03290     else
03291     {
03292       /* Send Slave Address and Memory Address */
03293       if (I2C_RequestMemoryRead(hi2c, DevAddress, MemAddress, MemAddSize, I2C_TIMEOUT_FLAG, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
03294       {
03295         return HAL_ERROR;
03296       }
03297 
03298       /* Clear ADDR flag */
03299       __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
03300 
03301       /* Generate Stop */
03302       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
03303 
03304       hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
03305 
03306       /* Process Unlocked */
03307       __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03308     }
03309 
03310     return HAL_OK;
03311   }
03312   else
03313   {
03314     return HAL_BUSY;
03315   }
03316 }
03317 
03318 /**
03319   * @brief  Checks if target device is ready for communication.
03320   * @note   This function is used with Memory devices
03321   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
03322   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
03323   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
03324   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
03325   * @param  Trials Number of trials
03326   * @param  Timeout Timeout duration
03327   * @retval HAL status
03328   */
03329 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_IsDeviceReady(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint32_t Trials, uint32_t Timeout)
03330 {
03331   /* Get tick */
03332   uint32_t tickstart = HAL_GetTick();
03333   uint32_t I2C_Trials = 1U;
03334   FlagStatus tmp1;
03335   FlagStatus tmp2;
03336 
03337   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
03338   {
03339     /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
03340     if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY, SET, I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
03341     {
03342       return HAL_BUSY;
03343     }
03344 
03345     /* Process Locked */
03346     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
03347 
03348     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
03349     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
03350     {
03351       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
03352       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
03353     }
03354 
03355     /* Disable Pos */
03356     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
03357 
03358     hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY;
03359     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
03360     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
03361 
03362     do
03363     {
03364       /* Generate Start */
03365       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
03366 
03367       /* Wait until SB flag is set */
03368       if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_SB, RESET, Timeout, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
03369       {
03370         return HAL_ERROR;
03371       }
03372 
03373       /* Send slave address */
03374       hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_7BIT_ADD_WRITE(DevAddress);
03375 
03376       /* Wait until ADDR or AF flag are set */
03377       /* Get tick */
03378       tickstart = HAL_GetTick();
03379 
03380       tmp1 = __HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_ADDR);
03381       tmp2 = __HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_AF);
03382       while ((hi2c->State != HAL_I2C_STATE_TIMEOUT) && (tmp1 == RESET) && (tmp2 == RESET))
03383       {
03384         if (((HAL_GetTick() - tickstart) > Timeout) || (Timeout == 0U))
03385         {
03386           hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_TIMEOUT;
03387         }
03388         tmp1 = __HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_ADDR);
03389         tmp2 = __HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_AF);
03390       }
03391 
03392       hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
03393 
03394       /* Check if the ADDR flag has been set */
03395       if (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_ADDR) == SET)
03396       {
03397         /* Generate Stop */
03398         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
03399 
03400         /* Clear ADDR Flag */
03401         __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
03402 
03403         /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
03404         if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY, SET, I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
03405         {
03406           return HAL_ERROR;
03407         }
03408 
03409         hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
03410 
03411         /* Process Unlocked */
03412         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03413 
03414         return HAL_OK;
03415       }
03416       else
03417       {
03418         /* Generate Stop */
03419         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
03420 
03421         /* Clear AF Flag */
03422         __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_AF);
03423 
03424         /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
03425         if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY, SET, I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG, tickstart) != HAL_OK)
03426         {
03427           return HAL_ERROR;
03428         }
03429       }
03430 
03431       /* Increment Trials */
03432       I2C_Trials++;
03433     }
03434     while (I2C_Trials < Trials);
03435 
03436     hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
03437 
03438     /* Process Unlocked */
03439     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03440 
03441     return HAL_ERROR;
03442   }
03443   else
03444   {
03445     return HAL_BUSY;
03446   }
03447 }
03448 
03449 /**
03450   * @brief  Sequential transmit in master I2C mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode with Interrupt.
03451   * @note   This interface allow to manage repeated start condition when a direction change during transfer
03452   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
03453   *         the configuration information for the specified I2C.
03454   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
03455   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
03456   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
03457   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
03458   * @param  XferOptions Options of Transfer, value of @ref I2C_XferOptions_definition
03459   * @retval HAL status
03460   */
03461 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Transmit_IT(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size, uint32_t XferOptions)
03462 {
03463   __IO uint32_t Prev_State = 0x00U;
03464   __IO uint32_t count      = 0x00U;
03465 
03466   /* Check the parameters */
03467   assert_param(IS_I2C_TRANSFER_OPTIONS_REQUEST(XferOptions));
03468 
03469   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
03470   {
03471     /* Check Busy Flag only if FIRST call of Master interface */
03472     if ((XferOptions == I2C_FIRST_AND_LAST_FRAME) || (XferOptions == I2C_FIRST_FRAME))
03473     {
03474       /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
03475       count = I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG * (SystemCoreClock / 25U / 1000U);
03476       do
03477       {
03478         count--;
03479         if (count == 0U)
03480         {
03481           hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
03482           hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
03483           hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
03484           hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_TIMEOUT;
03485 
03486           /* Process Unlocked */
03487           __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03488 
03489           return HAL_ERROR;
03490         }
03491       }
03492       while (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY) != RESET);
03493     }
03494 
03495     /* Process Locked */
03496     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
03497 
03498     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
03499     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
03500     {
03501       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
03502       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
03503     }
03504 
03505     /* Disable Pos */
03506     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
03507 
03508     hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX;
03509     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_MASTER;
03510     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
03511 
03512     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
03513     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
03514     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
03515     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
03516     hi2c->XferOptions = XferOptions;
03517     hi2c->Devaddress  = DevAddress;
03518 
03519     Prev_State = hi2c->PreviousState;
03520 
03521     /* If transfer direction not change and there is no request to start another frame, do not generate Restart Condition */
03522     /* Mean Previous state is same as current state */
03523     if ((Prev_State != I2C_STATE_MASTER_BUSY_TX) || (IS_I2C_TRANSFER_OTHER_OPTIONS_REQUEST(XferOptions) == 1))
03524     {
03525       /* Generate Start */
03526       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
03527     }
03528 
03529     /* Process Unlocked */
03530     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03531 
03532     /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
03533     to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
03534     process unlock */
03535 
03536     /* Enable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
03537     __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
03538 
03539     return HAL_OK;
03540   }
03541   else
03542   {
03543     return HAL_BUSY;
03544   }
03545 }
03546 
03547 /**
03548   * @brief  Sequential transmit in master I2C mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode with DMA.
03549   * @note   This interface allow to manage repeated start condition when a direction change during transfer
03550   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
03551   *         the configuration information for the specified I2C.
03552   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
03553   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
03554   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
03555   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
03556   * @param  XferOptions Options of Transfer, value of @ref I2C_XferOptions_definition
03557   * @retval HAL status
03558   */
03559 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Transmit_DMA(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size, uint32_t XferOptions)
03560 {
03561   __IO uint32_t Prev_State = 0x00U;
03562   __IO uint32_t count      = 0x00U;
03563   HAL_StatusTypeDef dmaxferstatus;
03564 
03565   /* Check the parameters */
03566   assert_param(IS_I2C_TRANSFER_OPTIONS_REQUEST(XferOptions));
03567 
03568   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
03569   {
03570     /* Check Busy Flag only if FIRST call of Master interface */
03571     if ((XferOptions == I2C_FIRST_AND_LAST_FRAME) || (XferOptions == I2C_FIRST_FRAME))
03572     {
03573       /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
03574       count = I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG * (SystemCoreClock / 25U / 1000U);
03575       do
03576       {
03577         count--;
03578         if (count == 0U)
03579         {
03580           hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
03581           hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
03582           hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
03583           hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_TIMEOUT;
03584 
03585           /* Process Unlocked */
03586           __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03587 
03588           return HAL_ERROR;
03589         }
03590       }
03591       while (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY) != RESET);
03592     }
03593 
03594     /* Process Locked */
03595     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
03596 
03597     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
03598     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
03599     {
03600       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
03601       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
03602     }
03603 
03604     /* Disable Pos */
03605     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
03606 
03607     hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX;
03608     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_MASTER;
03609     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
03610 
03611     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
03612     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
03613     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
03614     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
03615     hi2c->XferOptions = XferOptions;
03616     hi2c->Devaddress  = DevAddress;
03617 
03618     Prev_State = hi2c->PreviousState;
03619 
03620     if (hi2c->XferSize > 0U)
03621     {
03622       /* Set the I2C DMA transfer complete callback */
03623       hi2c->hdmatx->XferCpltCallback = I2C_DMAXferCplt;
03624 
03625       /* Set the DMA error callback */
03626       hi2c->hdmatx->XferErrorCallback = I2C_DMAError;
03627 
03628       /* Set the unused DMA callbacks to NULL */
03629       hi2c->hdmatx->XferHalfCpltCallback = NULL;
03630       hi2c->hdmatx->XferAbortCallback = NULL;
03631 
03632       /* Enable the DMA channel */
03633       dmaxferstatus = HAL_DMA_Start_IT(hi2c->hdmatx, (uint32_t)hi2c->pBuffPtr, (uint32_t)&hi2c->Instance->DR, hi2c->XferSize);
03634 
03635       if (dmaxferstatus == HAL_OK)
03636       {
03637         /* Enable Acknowledge */
03638         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
03639 
03640         /* If transfer direction not change and there is no request to start another frame, do not generate Restart Condition */
03641         /* Mean Previous state is same as current state */
03642         if ((Prev_State != I2C_STATE_MASTER_BUSY_TX) || (IS_I2C_TRANSFER_OTHER_OPTIONS_REQUEST(XferOptions) == 1))
03643         {
03644           /* Generate Start */
03645           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
03646         }
03647 
03648         /* Process Unlocked */
03649         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03650 
03651         /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
03652         to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
03653         process unlock */
03654 
03655         /* If XferOptions is not associated to a new frame, mean no start bit is request, enable directly the DMA request */
03656         /* In other cases, DMA request is enabled after Slave address treatment in IRQHandler */
03657         if ((XferOptions == I2C_NEXT_FRAME) || (XferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME) || (XferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME_NO_STOP))
03658         {
03659           /* Enable DMA Request */
03660           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN);
03661         }
03662 
03663         /* Enable EVT and ERR interrupt */
03664         __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_ERR);
03665       }
03666       else
03667       {
03668         /* Update I2C state */
03669         hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
03670         hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
03671 
03672         /* Update I2C error code */
03673         hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_DMA;
03674 
03675         /* Process Unlocked */
03676         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03677 
03678         return HAL_ERROR;
03679       }
03680     }
03681     else
03682     {
03683       /* Enable Acknowledge */
03684       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
03685 
03686       /* If transfer direction not change and there is no request to start another frame, do not generate Restart Condition */
03687       /* Mean Previous state is same as current state */
03688       if ((Prev_State != I2C_STATE_MASTER_BUSY_TX) || (IS_I2C_TRANSFER_OTHER_OPTIONS_REQUEST(XferOptions) == 1))
03689       {
03690         /* Generate Start */
03691         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
03692       }
03693 
03694       /* Process Unlocked */
03695       __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03696 
03697       /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
03698       to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
03699       process unlock */
03700 
03701       /* Enable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
03702       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
03703     }
03704 
03705     return HAL_OK;
03706   }
03707   else
03708   {
03709     return HAL_BUSY;
03710   }
03711 }
03712 
03713 /**
03714   * @brief  Sequential receive in master I2C mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode with Interrupt
03715   * @note   This interface allow to manage repeated start condition when a direction change during transfer
03716   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
03717   *         the configuration information for the specified I2C.
03718   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
03719   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
03720   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
03721   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
03722   * @param  XferOptions Options of Transfer, value of @ref I2C_XferOptions_definition
03723   * @retval HAL status
03724   */
03725 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Receive_IT(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size, uint32_t XferOptions)
03726 {
03727   __IO uint32_t Prev_State = 0x00U;
03728   __IO uint32_t count = 0U;
03729   uint32_t enableIT = (I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
03730 
03731   /* Check the parameters */
03732   assert_param(IS_I2C_TRANSFER_OPTIONS_REQUEST(XferOptions));
03733 
03734   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
03735   {
03736     /* Check Busy Flag only if FIRST call of Master interface */
03737     if ((XferOptions == I2C_FIRST_AND_LAST_FRAME) || (XferOptions == I2C_FIRST_FRAME))
03738     {
03739       /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
03740       count = I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG * (SystemCoreClock / 25U / 1000U);
03741       do
03742       {
03743         count--;
03744         if (count == 0U)
03745         {
03746           hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
03747           hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
03748           hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
03749           hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_TIMEOUT;
03750 
03751           /* Process Unlocked */
03752           __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03753 
03754           return HAL_ERROR;
03755         }
03756       }
03757       while (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY) != RESET);
03758     }
03759 
03760     /* Process Locked */
03761     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
03762 
03763     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
03764     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
03765     {
03766       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
03767       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
03768     }
03769 
03770     /* Disable Pos */
03771     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
03772 
03773     hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX;
03774     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_MASTER;
03775     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
03776 
03777     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
03778     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
03779     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
03780     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
03781     hi2c->XferOptions = XferOptions;
03782     hi2c->Devaddress  = DevAddress;
03783 
03784     Prev_State = hi2c->PreviousState;
03785 
03786     if ((hi2c->XferCount == 2U) && ((XferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME) || (XferOptions == I2C_OTHER_AND_LAST_FRAME) || (XferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME_NO_STOP)))
03787     {
03788       /* Disable Acknowledge */
03789       CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
03790 
03791       /* Enable Pos */
03792       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
03793 
03794       /* Remove Enabling of IT_BUF, mean RXNE treatment, treat the 2 bytes through BTF */
03795       enableIT &= ~I2C_IT_BUF;
03796     }
03797     else
03798     {
03799       /* Enable Acknowledge */
03800       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
03801     }
03802 
03803     /* If transfer direction not change and there is no request to start another frame, do not generate Restart Condition */
03804     /* Mean Previous state is same as current state */
03805     if ((Prev_State != I2C_STATE_MASTER_BUSY_RX) || (IS_I2C_TRANSFER_OTHER_OPTIONS_REQUEST(XferOptions) == 1))
03806     {
03807       /* Generate Start */
03808       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
03809     }
03810 
03811     /* Process Unlocked */
03812     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03813 
03814     /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
03815     to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
03816     process unlock */
03817 
03818     /* Enable interrupts */
03819     __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, enableIT);
03820 
03821     return HAL_OK;
03822   }
03823   else
03824   {
03825     return HAL_BUSY;
03826   }
03827 }
03828 
03829 /**
03830   * @brief  Sequential receive in master mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode with DMA
03831   * @note   This interface allow to manage repeated start condition when a direction change during transfer
03832   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
03833   *         the configuration information for the specified I2C.
03834   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
03835   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
03836   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
03837   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
03838   * @param  XferOptions Options of Transfer, value of @ref I2C_XferOptions_definition
03839   * @retval HAL status
03840   */
03841 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Master_Seq_Receive_DMA(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size, uint32_t XferOptions)
03842 {
03843   __IO uint32_t Prev_State = 0x00U;
03844   __IO uint32_t count = 0U;
03845   uint32_t enableIT = (I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
03846   HAL_StatusTypeDef dmaxferstatus;
03847 
03848   /* Check the parameters */
03849   assert_param(IS_I2C_TRANSFER_OPTIONS_REQUEST(XferOptions));
03850 
03851   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
03852   {
03853     /* Check Busy Flag only if FIRST call of Master interface */
03854     if ((XferOptions == I2C_FIRST_AND_LAST_FRAME) || (XferOptions == I2C_FIRST_FRAME))
03855     {
03856       /* Wait until BUSY flag is reset */
03857       count = I2C_TIMEOUT_BUSY_FLAG * (SystemCoreClock / 25U / 1000U);
03858       do
03859       {
03860         count--;
03861         if (count == 0U)
03862         {
03863           hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
03864           hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
03865           hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
03866           hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_TIMEOUT;
03867 
03868           /* Process Unlocked */
03869           __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03870 
03871           return HAL_ERROR;
03872         }
03873       }
03874       while (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BUSY) != RESET);
03875     }
03876 
03877     /* Process Locked */
03878     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
03879 
03880     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
03881     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
03882     {
03883       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
03884       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
03885     }
03886 
03887     /* Disable Pos */
03888     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
03889 
03890     /* Clear Last DMA bit */
03891     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_LAST);
03892 
03893     hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX;
03894     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_MASTER;
03895     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
03896 
03897     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
03898     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
03899     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
03900     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
03901     hi2c->XferOptions = XferOptions;
03902     hi2c->Devaddress  = DevAddress;
03903 
03904     Prev_State = hi2c->PreviousState;
03905 
03906     if (hi2c->XferSize > 0U)
03907     {
03908       if ((hi2c->XferCount == 2U) && ((XferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME) || (XferOptions == I2C_OTHER_AND_LAST_FRAME) || (XferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME_NO_STOP)))
03909       {
03910         /* Disable Acknowledge */
03911         CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
03912 
03913         /* Enable Pos */
03914         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
03915 
03916         /* Enable Last DMA bit */
03917         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_LAST);
03918       }
03919       else
03920       {
03921         /* Enable Acknowledge */
03922         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
03923 
03924         if ((XferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME) || (XferOptions == I2C_OTHER_AND_LAST_FRAME) || (XferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME_NO_STOP))
03925         {
03926           /* Enable Last DMA bit */
03927           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_LAST);
03928         }
03929       }
03930 
03931       /* Set the I2C DMA transfer complete callback */
03932       hi2c->hdmarx->XferCpltCallback = I2C_DMAXferCplt;
03933 
03934       /* Set the DMA error callback */
03935       hi2c->hdmarx->XferErrorCallback = I2C_DMAError;
03936 
03937       /* Set the unused DMA callbacks to NULL */
03938       hi2c->hdmarx->XferHalfCpltCallback = NULL;
03939       hi2c->hdmarx->XferAbortCallback = NULL;
03940 
03941       /* Enable the DMA channel */
03942       dmaxferstatus = HAL_DMA_Start_IT(hi2c->hdmarx, (uint32_t)&hi2c->Instance->DR, (uint32_t)hi2c->pBuffPtr, hi2c->XferSize);
03943 
03944       if (dmaxferstatus == HAL_OK)
03945       {
03946         /* If transfer direction not change and there is no request to start another frame, do not generate Restart Condition */
03947         /* Mean Previous state is same as current state */
03948         if ((Prev_State != I2C_STATE_MASTER_BUSY_RX) || (IS_I2C_TRANSFER_OTHER_OPTIONS_REQUEST(XferOptions) == 1))
03949         {
03950           /* Generate Start */
03951           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
03952         }
03953 
03954         /* Process Unlocked */
03955         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03956 
03957         /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
03958         to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
03959         process unlock */
03960 
03961         /* If XferOptions is not associated to a new frame, mean no start bit is request, enable directly the DMA request */
03962         /* In other cases, DMA request is enabled after Slave address treatment in IRQHandler */
03963         if ((XferOptions == I2C_NEXT_FRAME) || (XferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME) || (XferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME_NO_STOP))
03964         {
03965           /* Enable DMA Request */
03966           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN);
03967         }
03968 
03969         /* Enable EVT and ERR interrupt */
03970         __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_ERR);
03971       }
03972       else
03973       {
03974         /* Update I2C state */
03975         hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
03976         hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
03977 
03978         /* Update I2C error code */
03979         hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_DMA;
03980 
03981         /* Process Unlocked */
03982         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
03983 
03984         return HAL_ERROR;
03985       }
03986     }
03987     else
03988     {
03989       /* Enable Acknowledge */
03990       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
03991 
03992       /* If transfer direction not change and there is no request to start another frame, do not generate Restart Condition */
03993       /* Mean Previous state is same as current state */
03994       if ((Prev_State != I2C_STATE_MASTER_BUSY_RX) || (IS_I2C_TRANSFER_OTHER_OPTIONS_REQUEST(XferOptions) == 1))
03995       {
03996         /* Generate Start */
03997         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
03998       }
03999 
04000       /* Process Unlocked */
04001       __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
04002 
04003       /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
04004       to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
04005       process unlock */
04006 
04007       /* Enable interrupts */
04008       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, enableIT);
04009     }
04010     return HAL_OK;
04011   }
04012   else
04013   {
04014     return HAL_BUSY;
04015   }
04016 }
04017 
04018 /**
04019   * @brief  Sequential transmit in slave mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode with Interrupt
04020   * @note   This interface allow to manage repeated start condition when a direction change during transfer
04021   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
04022   *         the configuration information for the specified I2C.
04023   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
04024   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
04025   * @param  XferOptions Options of Transfer, value of @ref I2C_XferOptions_definition
04026   * @retval HAL status
04027   */
04028 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Slave_Seq_Transmit_IT(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size, uint32_t XferOptions)
04029 {
04030   /* Check the parameters */
04031   assert_param(IS_I2C_TRANSFER_OPTIONS_REQUEST(XferOptions));
04032 
04033   if (((uint32_t)hi2c->State & (uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN) == (uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN)
04034   {
04035     if ((pData == NULL) || (Size == 0U))
04036     {
04037       return  HAL_ERROR;
04038     }
04039 
04040     /* Process Locked */
04041     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
04042 
04043     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
04044     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
04045     {
04046       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
04047       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
04048     }
04049 
04050     /* Disable Pos */
04051     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
04052 
04053     hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX_LISTEN;
04054     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_SLAVE;
04055     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
04056 
04057     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
04058     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
04059     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
04060     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
04061     hi2c->XferOptions = XferOptions;
04062 
04063     /* Clear ADDR flag */
04064     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
04065 
04066     /* Process Unlocked */
04067     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
04068 
04069     /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
04070               to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
04071               process unlock */
04072 
04073     /* Enable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
04074     __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
04075 
04076     return HAL_OK;
04077   }
04078   else
04079   {
04080     return HAL_BUSY;
04081   }
04082 }
04083 
04084 /**
04085   * @brief  Sequential transmit in slave mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode with DMA
04086   * @note   This interface allow to manage repeated start condition when a direction change during transfer
04087   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
04088   *         the configuration information for the specified I2C.
04089   * @param  pData Pointer to data buffer
04090   * @param  Size Amount of data to be sent
04091   * @param  XferOptions Options of Transfer, value of @ref I2C_XferOptions_definition
04092   * @retval HAL status
04093   */
04094 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Slave_Seq_Transmit_DMA(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint8_t *pData, uint16_t Size, uint32_t XferOptions)
04095 {
04096   HAL_StatusTypeDef dmaxferstatus;
04097 
04098   /* Check the parameters */
04099   assert_param(IS_I2C_TRANSFER_OPTIONS_REQUEST(XferOptions));
04100 
04101   if (((uint32_t)hi2c->State & (uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN) == (uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN)
04102   {
04103     if ((pData == NULL) || (Size == 0U))
04104     {
04105       return  HAL_ERROR;
04106     }
04107 
04108     /* Process Locked */
04109     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
04110 
04111     /* Disable Interrupts, to prevent preemption during treatment in case of multicall */
04112     __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_ERR);
04113 
04114     /* I2C cannot manage full duplex exchange so disable previous IT enabled if any */
04115     /* and then toggle the HAL slave RX state to TX state */
04116     if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX_LISTEN)
04117     {
04118       if ((hi2c->Instance->CR2 & I2C_CR2_DMAEN) == I2C_CR2_DMAEN)
04119       {
04120         /* Abort DMA Xfer if any */
04121         if (hi2c->hdmarx != NULL)
04122         {
04123           CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN);
04124 
04125           /* Set the I2C DMA Abort callback :
04126            will lead to call HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback() at end of DMA abort procedure */
04127           hi2c->hdmarx->XferAbortCallback = I2C_DMAAbort;
04128 
04129           /* Abort DMA RX */
04130           if (HAL_DMA_Abort_IT(hi2c->hdmarx) != HAL_OK)
04131           {
04132             /* Call Directly XferAbortCallback function in case of error */
04133             hi2c->hdmarx->XferAbortCallback(hi2c->hdmarx);
04134           }
04135         }
04136       }
04137     }
04138     else if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX_LISTEN)
04139     {
04140       if ((hi2c->Instance->CR2 & I2C_CR2_DMAEN) == I2C_CR2_DMAEN)
04141       {
04142         CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN);
04143 
04144         /* Abort DMA Xfer if any */
04145         if (hi2c->hdmatx != NULL)
04146         {
04147           /* Set the I2C DMA Abort callback :
04148            will lead to call HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback() at end of DMA abort procedure */
04149           hi2c->hdmatx->XferAbortCallback = I2C_DMAAbort;
04150 
04151           /* Abort DMA TX */
04152           if (HAL_DMA_Abort_IT(hi2c->hdmatx) != HAL_OK)
04153           {
04154             /* Call Directly XferAbortCallback function in case of error */
04155             hi2c->hdmatx->XferAbortCallback(hi2c->hdmatx);
04156           }
04157         }
04158       }
04159     }
04160     else
04161     {
04162       /* Nothing to do */
04163     }
04164 
04165     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
04166     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
04167     {
04168       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
04169       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
04170     }
04171 
04172     /* Disable Pos */
04173     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
04174 
04175     hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX_LISTEN;
04176     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_SLAVE;
04177     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
04178 
04179     /* Prepare transfer parameters */
04180     hi2c->pBuffPtr    = pData;
04181     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;
04182     hi2c->XferSize    = hi2c->XferCount;
04183     hi2c->XferOptions = XferOptions;
04184 
04185     /* Set the I2C DMA transfer complete callback */
04186     hi2c->hdmatx->XferCpltCallback = I2C_DMAXferCplt;
04187 
04188     /* Set the DMA error callback */
04189     hi2c->hdmatx->XferErrorCallback = I2C_DMAError;
04190 
04191     /* Set the unused DMA callbacks to NULL */
04192     hi2c->hdmatx->XferHalfCpltCallback = NULL;
04193     hi2c->hdmatx->XferAbortCallback = NULL;
04194 
04195     /* Enable the DMA channel */
04196     dmaxferstatus = HAL_DMA_Start_IT(hi2c->hdmatx, (uint32_t)hi2c->pBuffPtr, (uint32_t)&hi2c->Instance->DR, hi2c->XferSize);
04197 
04198     if (dmaxferstatus == HAL_OK)
04199     {
04200       /* Enable Address Acknowledge */
04201       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
04202 
04203       /* Clear ADDR flag */
04204       __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
04205 
04206       /* Process Unlocked */
04207       __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
04208 
04209       /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
04210       to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
04211       process unlock */
04212       /* Enable EVT and ERR interrupt */
04213       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_ERR);
04214 
04215       /* Enable DMA Request */
04216       hi2c->Instance->CR2 |= I2C_CR2_DMAEN;
04217 
04218       return HAL_OK;
04219     }
04220     else
04221     {
04222       /* Update I2C state */
04223       hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
04224       hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
04225 
04226       /* Update I2C error code */
04227       hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_DMA;
04228 
04229       /* Process Unlocked */
04230       __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
04231 
04232       return HAL_ERROR;
04233     }
04234   }
04235   else
04236   {
04237     return HAL_BUSY;
04238   }
04239 }

04241 /**
04242   * @brief  Sequential receive in slave mode an amount of data in non-blocking mode with Interrupt
04243   * @note   This interface allow to manage repeated start condition when a direction change during transfer
04244   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
04245   *         the configuration information for the specified I2C.

04259     {
04260       return  HAL_ERROR;
04261     }
04262

04264     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
04265

04275

04277     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_SLAVE;

04279

04282     hi2c->XferCount   = Size;

04284     hi2c->XferOptions = XferOptions;
04285

04287     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
04288 
04289     /* Process Unlocked */
04290     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
04291 
04292     /* Note : The I2C interrupts must be enabled after unlocking current process
04293               to avoid the risk of I2C interrupt handle execution before current
04294               process unlock */
04295 
04296     /* Enable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
04297     __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
04298 
04299     return HAL_OK;
04300   }
04301   else
04302   {
04303     return HAL_BUSY;
04304   }

04372           hi2c->hdmatx->XferAbortCallback = I2C_DMAAbort;
04373

04376           {

04380         }
04381       }

04383     else

04385       /* Nothing to do */
04386     }
04387 
04388     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
04389     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
04390     {

04397

04399     hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_SLAVE;
04400     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;

04410

04419     dmaxferstatus = HAL_DMA_Start_IT(hi2c->hdmarx, (uint32_t)&hi2c->Instance->DR, (uint32_t)hi2c->pBuffPtr, hi2c->XferSize);
04420 
04421     if (dmaxferstatus == HAL_OK)
04422     {
04423       /* Enable Address Acknowledge */
04424       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
04425

04428

04434

04437       process unlock */

04440 
04441       return HAL_OK;
04442     }
04443     else
04444     {
04445       /* Update I2C state */
04446       hi2c->State     = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
04447       hi2c->Mode      = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
04448 
04449       /* Update I2C error code */
04450       hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_DMA;
04451 
04452       /* Process Unlocked */
04453       __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
04454 
04455       return HAL_ERROR;
04456     }
04457   }
04458   else
04459   {
04460     return HAL_BUSY;
04461   }
04462 }

04464 /**
04465   * @brief  Enable the Address listen mode with Interrupt.
04466   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
04467   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
04468   * @retval HAL status
04469   */
04470 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_EnableListen_IT(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
04471 {
04472   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_READY)
04473   {
04474     hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN;
04475 
04476     /* Check if the I2C is already enabled */
04477     if ((hi2c->Instance->CR1 & I2C_CR1_PE) != I2C_CR1_PE)
04478     {
04479       /* Enable I2C peripheral */
04480       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
04481     }
04482 
04483     /* Enable Address Acknowledge */
04484     SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
04485 
04486     /* Enable EVT and ERR interrupt */
04487     __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_ERR);
04488 
04489     return HAL_OK;
04490   }
04491   else
04492   {
04493     return HAL_BUSY;
04494   }
04495 }
04496 
04497 /**
04498   * @brief  Disable the Address listen mode with Interrupt.
04499   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
04500   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
04501   * @retval HAL status
04502   */
04503 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_DisableListen_IT(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
04504 {
04505   /* Declaration of tmp to prevent undefined behavior of volatile usage */
04506   uint32_t tmp;
04507 
04508   /* Disable Address listen mode only if a transfer is not ongoing */
04509   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN)
04510   {
04511     tmp = (uint32_t)(hi2c->State) & I2C_STATE_MSK;
04512     hi2c->PreviousState = tmp | (uint32_t)(hi2c->Mode);
04513     hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
04514     hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
04515 
04516     /* Disable Address Acknowledge */
04517     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
04518 
04519     /* Disable EVT and ERR interrupt */
04520     __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_ERR);
04521 
04522     return HAL_OK;
04523   }
04524   else
04525   {
04526     return HAL_BUSY;
04527   }
04528 }
04529 
04530 /**
04531   * @brief  Abort a master I2C IT or DMA process communication with Interrupt.
04532   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
04533   *         the configuration information for the specified I2C.
04534   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
04535   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
04536   * @retval HAL status
04537   */
04538 HAL_StatusTypeDef HAL_I2C_Master_Abort_IT(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress)
04539 {
04540   /* Prevent unused argument(s) compilation warning */
04541   UNUSED(DevAddress);
04542 
04543   /* Abort Master transfer during Receive or Transmit process    */
04544   if (hi2c->Mode == HAL_I2C_MODE_MASTER)
04545   {
04546     /* Process Locked */
04547     __HAL_LOCK(hi2c);
04548 
04549     hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_NONE;
04550     hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_ABORT;
04551 
04552     /* Disable Acknowledge */
04553     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
04554 
04555     /* Generate Stop */
04556     SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
04557 
04558     hi2c->XferCount = 0U;
04559 
04560     /* Disable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
04561     __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
04562 
04563     /* Process Unlocked */
04564     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
04565 
04566     /* Call the corresponding callback to inform upper layer of End of Transfer */
04567     I2C_ITError(hi2c);
04568 
04569     return HAL_OK;
04570   }
04571   else
04572   {
04573     /* Wrong usage of abort function */
04574     /* This function should be used only in case of abort monitored by master device */
04575     return HAL_ERROR;
04576   }
04577 }
04578 
04579 /**
04580   * @}
04581   */
04582 
04583 /** @defgroup I2C_IRQ_Handler_and_Callbacks IRQ Handler and Callbacks
04584  * @{
04585  */
04586 
04587 /**
04588   * @brief  This function handles I2C event interrupt request.
04589   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
04590   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
04591   * @retval None
04592   */
04593 void HAL_I2C_EV_IRQHandler(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
04594 {
04595   uint32_t sr1itflags;
04596   uint32_t sr2itflags               = 0U;
04597   uint32_t itsources                = READ_REG(hi2c->Instance->CR2);
04598   uint32_t CurrentXferOptions       = hi2c->XferOptions;
04599   HAL_I2C_ModeTypeDef CurrentMode   = hi2c->Mode;
04600   HAL_I2C_StateTypeDef CurrentState = hi2c->State;
04601 
04602   /* Master or Memory mode selected */
04603   if ((CurrentMode == HAL_I2C_MODE_MASTER) || (CurrentMode == HAL_I2C_MODE_MEM))
04604   {
04605     sr2itflags   = READ_REG(hi2c->Instance->SR2);
04606     sr1itflags   = READ_REG(hi2c->Instance->SR1);
04607 
04608     /* Exit IRQ event until Start Bit detected in case of Other frame requested */
04609     if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_SB) == RESET) && (IS_I2C_TRANSFER_OTHER_OPTIONS_REQUEST(CurrentXferOptions) == 1U))
04610     {
04611       return;
04612     }
04613 
04614     /* SB Set ----------------------------------------------------------------*/
04615     if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_SB) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_EVT) != RESET))
04616     {
04617       /* Convert OTHER_xxx XferOptions if any */
04618       I2C_ConvertOtherXferOptions(hi2c);
04619 
04620       I2C_Master_SB(hi2c);
04621     }
04622     /* ADD10 Set -------------------------------------------------------------*/
04623     else if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_ADD10) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_EVT) != RESET))
04624     {
04625       I2C_Master_ADD10(hi2c);
04626     }
04627     /* ADDR Set --------------------------------------------------------------*/
04628     else if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_ADDR) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_EVT) != RESET))
04629     {
04630       I2C_Master_ADDR(hi2c);
04631     }
04632     /* I2C in mode Transmitter -----------------------------------------------*/
04633     else if (I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr2itflags, I2C_FLAG_TRA) != RESET)
04634     {
04635       /* Do not check buffer and BTF flag if a Xfer DMA is on going */
04636       if (READ_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN) != I2C_CR2_DMAEN)
04637       {
04638         /* TXE set and BTF reset -----------------------------------------------*/
04639         if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_TXE) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_BUF) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_BTF) == RESET))
04640         {
04641           I2C_MasterTransmit_TXE(hi2c);
04642         }
04643         /* BTF set -------------------------------------------------------------*/
04644         else if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_BTF) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_EVT) != RESET))
04645         {
04646           I2C_MasterTransmit_BTF(hi2c);
04647         }
04648         else
04649         {
04650           /* Do nothing */
04651         }
04652       }
04653     }
04654     /* I2C in mode Receiver --------------------------------------------------*/
04655     else
04656     {
04657       /* Do not check buffer and BTF flag if a Xfer DMA is on going */
04658       if (READ_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN) != I2C_CR2_DMAEN)
04659       {
04660         /* RXNE set and BTF reset -----------------------------------------------*/
04661         if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_RXNE) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_BUF) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_BTF) == RESET))
04662         {
04663           I2C_MasterReceive_RXNE(hi2c);
04664         }
04665         /* BTF set -------------------------------------------------------------*/
04666         else if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_BTF) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_EVT) != RESET))
04667         {
04668           I2C_MasterReceive_BTF(hi2c);
04669         }
04670         else
04671         {
04672           /* Do nothing */
04673         }
04674       }
04675     }
04676   }
04677   /* Slave mode selected */
04678   else
04679   {
04680     /* If an error is detected, read only SR1 register to prevent */
04681     /* a clear of ADDR flags by reading SR2 after reading SR1 in Error treatment */
04682     if (hi2c->ErrorCode != HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE)
04683     {
04684       sr1itflags   = READ_REG(hi2c->Instance->SR1);
04685     }
04686     else
04687     {
04688       sr2itflags   = READ_REG(hi2c->Instance->SR2);
04689       sr1itflags   = READ_REG(hi2c->Instance->SR1);
04690     }
04691 
04692     /* ADDR set --------------------------------------------------------------*/
04693     if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_ADDR) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_EVT) != RESET))
04694     {
04695       /* Now time to read SR2, this will clear ADDR flag automatically */
04696       if (hi2c->ErrorCode != HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE)
04697       {
04698         sr2itflags   = READ_REG(hi2c->Instance->SR2);
04699       }
04700       I2C_Slave_ADDR(hi2c, sr2itflags);
04701     }
04702     /* STOPF set --------------------------------------------------------------*/
04703     else if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_STOPF) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_EVT) != RESET))
04704     {
04705       I2C_Slave_STOPF(hi2c);
04706     }
04707     /* I2C in mode Transmitter -----------------------------------------------*/
04708     else if ((CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX) || (CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX_LISTEN))
04709     {
04710       /* TXE set and BTF reset -----------------------------------------------*/
04711       if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_TXE) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_BUF) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_BTF) == RESET))
04712       {
04713         I2C_SlaveTransmit_TXE(hi2c);
04714       }
04715       /* BTF set -------------------------------------------------------------*/
04716       else if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_BTF) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_EVT) != RESET))
04717       {
04718         I2C_SlaveTransmit_BTF(hi2c);
04719       }
04720       else
04721       {
04722         /* Do nothing */
04723       }
04724     }
04725     /* I2C in mode Receiver --------------------------------------------------*/
04726     else
04727     {
04728       /* RXNE set and BTF reset ----------------------------------------------*/
04729       if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_RXNE) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_BUF) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_BTF) == RESET))
04730       {
04731         I2C_SlaveReceive_RXNE(hi2c);
04732       }
04733       /* BTF set -------------------------------------------------------------*/
04734       else if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_BTF) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_EVT) != RESET))
04735       {
04736         I2C_SlaveReceive_BTF(hi2c);
04737       }
04738       else
04739       {
04740         /* Do nothing */
04741       }
04742     }
04743   }
04744 }
04745 
04746 /**
04747   * @brief  This function handles I2C error interrupt request.
04748   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
04749   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
04750   * @retval None
04751   */
04752 void HAL_I2C_ER_IRQHandler(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
04753 {
04754   HAL_I2C_ModeTypeDef tmp1;
04755   uint32_t tmp2;
04756   HAL_I2C_StateTypeDef tmp3;
04757   uint32_t tmp4;
04758   uint32_t sr1itflags = READ_REG(hi2c->Instance->SR1);
04759   uint32_t itsources  = READ_REG(hi2c->Instance->CR2);
04760   uint32_t error      = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
04761 
04762   /* I2C Bus error interrupt occurred ----------------------------------------*/
04763   if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_BERR) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_ERR) != RESET))
04764   {
04765     error |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_BERR;
04766 
04767     /* Clear BERR flag */
04768     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BERR);
04769 
04770     /* Workaround: Start cannot be generated after a misplaced Stop */
04771     SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_SWRST);
04772   }
04773 
04774   /* I2C Arbitration Lost error interrupt occurred ---------------------------*/
04775   if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_ARLO) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_ERR) != RESET))
04776   {
04777     error |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_ARLO;
04778 
04779     /* Clear ARLO flag */
04780     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_ARLO);
04781   }
04782 
04783   /* I2C Acknowledge failure error interrupt occurred ------------------------*/
04784   if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_AF) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_ERR) != RESET))
04785   {
04786     tmp1 = hi2c->Mode;
04787     tmp2 = hi2c->XferCount;
04788     tmp3 = hi2c->State;
04789     tmp4 = hi2c->PreviousState;
04790     if ((tmp1 == HAL_I2C_MODE_SLAVE) && (tmp2 == 0U) && \
04791         ((tmp3 == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX) || (tmp3 == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX_LISTEN) || \
04792          ((tmp3 == HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN) && (tmp4 == I2C_STATE_SLAVE_BUSY_TX))))
04793     {
04794       I2C_Slave_AF(hi2c);
04795     }
04796     else
04797     {
04798       /* Clear AF flag */
04799       __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_AF);
04800 
04801       error |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF;
04802 
04803       /* Do not generate a STOP in case of Slave receive non acknowledge during transfer (mean not at the end of transfer) */
04804       if (hi2c->Mode == HAL_I2C_MODE_MASTER)
04805       {
04806         /* Generate Stop */
04807         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
04808       }
04809     }
04810   }
04811 
04812   /* I2C Over-Run/Under-Run interrupt occurred -------------------------------*/
04813   if ((I2C_CHECK_FLAG(sr1itflags, I2C_FLAG_OVR) != RESET) && (I2C_CHECK_IT_SOURCE(itsources, I2C_IT_ERR) != RESET))
04814   {
04815     error |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_OVR;
04816     /* Clear OVR flag */
04817     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_OVR);
04818   }
04819 
04820   /* Call the Error Callback in case of Error detected -----------------------*/
04821   if (error != HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE)
04822   {
04823     hi2c->ErrorCode |= error;
04824     I2C_ITError(hi2c);
04825   }
04826 }

04994 
04995 /** @defgroup I2C_Exported_Functions_Group3 Peripheral State, Mode and Error functions
04996  *  @brief   Peripheral State, Mode and Error functions
04997   *
04998 @verbatim
04999  ===============================================================================
05000             ##### Peripheral State, Mode and Error functions #####
05001  ===============================================================================
05002     [..]
05003     This subsection permit to get in run-time the status of the peripheral
05004     and the data flow.
05005 
05006 @endverbatim
05007   * @{
05008   */
05009 
05010 /**
05011   * @brief  Return the I2C handle state.
05012   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
05013   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
05014   * @retval HAL state
05015   */
05016 HAL_I2C_StateTypeDef HAL_I2C_GetState(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
05017 {
05018   /* Return I2C handle state */
05019   return hi2c->State;
05020 }
05021 
05022 /**
05023   * @brief  Returns the I2C Master, Slave, Memory or no mode.
05024   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
05025   *         the configuration information for I2C module
05026   * @retval HAL mode
05027   */
05028 HAL_I2C_ModeTypeDef HAL_I2C_GetMode(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
05029 {
05030   return hi2c->Mode;
05031 }
05032 
05033 /**
05034   * @brief  Return the I2C error code.
05035   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
05036   *              the configuration information for the specified I2C.
05037   * @retval I2C Error Code
05038   */
05039 uint32_t HAL_I2C_GetError(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
05040 {
05041   return hi2c->ErrorCode;
05042 }
05043 
05044 /**
05045   * @}
05046   */
05047 
05048 /**
05049   * @}
05050   */

05053   * @{
05054   */
