05056 /**
05057   * @brief  Handle TXE flag for Master
05058   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
05059   *         the configuration information for I2C module
05060   * @retval None
05061   */
05062 static void I2C_MasterTransmit_TXE(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
05063 {
05064   /* Declaration of temporary variables to prevent undefined behavior of volatile usage */
05065   HAL_I2C_StateTypeDef CurrentState = hi2c->State;
05066   HAL_I2C_ModeTypeDef CurrentMode   = hi2c->Mode;
05067   uint32_t CurrentXferOptions       = hi2c->XferOptions;
05068 
05069   if ((hi2c->XferSize == 0U) && (CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX))
05070   {
05071     /* Call TxCpltCallback() directly if no stop mode is set */
05072     if ((CurrentXferOptions != I2C_FIRST_AND_LAST_FRAME) && (CurrentXferOptions != I2C_LAST_FRAME) && (CurrentXferOptions != I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME))
05073     {
05074       __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
05075 
05076       hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_MASTER_BUSY_TX;
05077       hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
05078       hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
05079 
05080 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
05081       hi2c->MasterTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05082 #else
05083       HAL_I2C_MasterTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05084 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
05085     }
05086     else /* Generate Stop condition then Call TxCpltCallback() */
05087     {
05088       /* Disable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
05089       __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
05090 
05091       /* Generate Stop */
05092       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
05093 
05094       hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_NONE;
05095       hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
05096 
05097       if (hi2c->Mode == HAL_I2C_MODE_MEM)
05098       {
05099         hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
05100 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
05101         hi2c->MemTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05102 #else
05103         HAL_I2C_MemTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05104 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
05105       }
05106       else
05107       {
05108         hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
05109 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
05110         hi2c->MasterTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05111 #else
05112         HAL_I2C_MasterTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05113 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
05114       }
05115     }
05116   }
05117   else if ((CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX) || \
05118            ((CurrentMode == HAL_I2C_MODE_MEM) && (CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX)))
05119   {
05120     if (hi2c->XferCount == 0U)
05121     {
05122       /* Disable BUF interrupt */
05123       __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_BUF);
05124     }
05125     else
05126     {
05127       if (hi2c->Mode == HAL_I2C_MODE_MEM)
05128       {
05129         if (hi2c->EventCount == 0U)
05130         {
05131           /* If Memory address size is 8Bit */
05132           if (hi2c->MemaddSize == I2C_MEMADD_SIZE_8BIT)
05133           {
05134             /* Send Memory Address */
05135             hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_MEM_ADD_LSB(hi2c->Memaddress);
05136 
05137             hi2c->EventCount += 2U;
05138           }
05139           /* If Memory address size is 16Bit */
05140           else
05141           {
05142             /* Send MSB of Memory Address */
05143             hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_MEM_ADD_MSB(hi2c->Memaddress);
05144 
05145             hi2c->EventCount++;
05146           }
05147         }
05148         else if (hi2c->EventCount == 1U)
05149         {
05150           /* Send LSB of Memory Address */
05151           hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_MEM_ADD_LSB(hi2c->Memaddress);
05152 
05153           hi2c->EventCount++;
05154         }
05155         else if (hi2c->EventCount == 2U)
05156         {
05157           if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX)
05158           {
05159             /* Generate Restart */
05160             hi2c->Instance->CR1 |= I2C_CR1_START;
05161           }
05162           else if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX)
05163           {
05164             /* Write data to DR */
05165             hi2c->Instance->DR = *hi2c->pBuffPtr;
05166 
05167             /* Increment Buffer pointer */
05168             hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
05169 
05170             /* Update counter */
05171             hi2c->XferCount--;
05172           }
05173           else
05174           {
05175             /* Do nothing */
05176           }
05177         }
05178         else
05179         {
05180           /* Do nothing */
05181         }
05182       }
05183       else
05184       {
05185         /* Write data to DR */
05186         hi2c->Instance->DR = *hi2c->pBuffPtr;
05187 
05188         /* Increment Buffer pointer */
05189         hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
05190 
05191         /* Update counter */
05192         hi2c->XferCount--;
05193       }
05194     }
05195   }
05196   else
05197   {
05198     /* Do nothing */
05199   }
05200 }
05201 
05202 /**
05203   * @brief  Handle BTF flag for Master transmitter
05204   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
05205   *         the configuration information for I2C module
05206   * @retval None
05207   */
05208 static void I2C_MasterTransmit_BTF(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
05209 {
05210   /* Declaration of temporary variables to prevent undefined behavior of volatile usage */
05211   uint32_t CurrentXferOptions = hi2c->XferOptions;
05212 
05213   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX)
05214   {
05215     if (hi2c->XferCount != 0U)
05216     {
05217       /* Write data to DR */
05218       hi2c->Instance->DR = *hi2c->pBuffPtr;
05219 
05220       /* Increment Buffer pointer */
05221       hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
05222 
05223       /* Update counter */
05224       hi2c->XferCount--;
05225     }
05226     else
05227     {
05228       /* Call TxCpltCallback() directly if no stop mode is set */
05229       if ((CurrentXferOptions != I2C_FIRST_AND_LAST_FRAME) && (CurrentXferOptions != I2C_LAST_FRAME) && (CurrentXferOptions != I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME))
05230       {
05231         __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
05232 
05233         hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_MASTER_BUSY_TX;
05234         hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
05235         hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
05236 
05237 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
05238         hi2c->MasterTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05239 #else
05240         HAL_I2C_MasterTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05241 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
05242       }
05243       else /* Generate Stop condition then Call TxCpltCallback() */
05244       {
05245         /* Disable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
05246         __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
05247 
05248         /* Generate Stop */
05249         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
05250 
05251         hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_NONE;
05252         hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
05253 
05254         if (hi2c->Mode == HAL_I2C_MODE_MEM)
05255         {
05256           hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
05257 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
05258           hi2c->MemTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05259 #else
05260           HAL_I2C_MemTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05261 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
05262         }
05263         else
05264         {
05265           hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
05266 
05267 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
05268           hi2c->MasterTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05269 #else
05270           HAL_I2C_MasterTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05271 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
05272         }
05273       }
05274     }
05275   }
05276 }
05277 
05278 /**
05279   * @brief  Handle RXNE flag for Master
05280   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
05281   *         the configuration information for I2C module
05282   * @retval None
05283   */
05284 static void I2C_MasterReceive_RXNE(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
05285 {
05286   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX)
05287   {
05288     uint32_t tmp;
05289 
05290     tmp = hi2c->XferCount;
05291     if (tmp > 3U)
05292     {
05293       /* Read data from DR */
05294       *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
05295 
05296       /* Increment Buffer pointer */
05297       hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
05298 
05299       /* Update counter */
05300       hi2c->XferCount--;
05301 
05302       if (hi2c->XferCount == (uint16_t)3)
05303       {
05304         /* Disable BUF interrupt, this help to treat correctly the last 4 bytes
05305         on BTF subroutine */
05306         /* Disable BUF interrupt */
05307         __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_BUF);
05308       }
05309     }
05310     else if ((hi2c->XferOptions != I2C_FIRST_AND_NEXT_FRAME) && ((tmp == 1U) || (tmp == 0U)))
05311     {
05312       /* Disable Acknowledge */
05313       CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
05314 
05315       /* Disable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
05316       __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
05317 
05318       /* Read data from DR */
05319       *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
05320 
05321       /* Increment Buffer pointer */
05322       hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
05323 
05324       /* Update counter */
05325       hi2c->XferCount--;
05326 
05327       hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
05328 
05329       if (hi2c->Mode == HAL_I2C_MODE_MEM)
05330       {
05331         hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
05332         hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_NONE;
05333 
05334 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
05335         hi2c->MemRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05336 #else
05337         HAL_I2C_MemRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05338 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
05339       }
05340       else
05341       {
05342         hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
05343         hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_MASTER_BUSY_RX;
05344 
05345 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
05346         hi2c->MasterRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05347 #else
05348         HAL_I2C_MasterRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05349 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
05350       }
05351     }
05352     else
05353     {
05354       /* Do nothing */
05355     }
05356   }
05357 }
05358 
05359 /**
05360   * @brief  Handle BTF flag for Master receiver
05361   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
05362   *         the configuration information for I2C module
05363   * @retval None
05364   */
05365 static void I2C_MasterReceive_BTF(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
05366 {
05367   /* Declaration of temporary variables to prevent undefined behavior of volatile usage */
05368   uint32_t CurrentXferOptions = hi2c->XferOptions;
05369 
05370   if (hi2c->XferCount == 4U)
05371   {
05372     /* Disable BUF interrupt, this help to treat correctly the last 2 bytes
05373        on BTF subroutine if there is a reception delay between N-1 and N byte */
05374     __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_BUF);
05375 
05376     /* Read data from DR */
05377     *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
05378 
05379     /* Increment Buffer pointer */
05380     hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
05381 
05382     /* Update counter */
05383     hi2c->XferCount--;
05384   }
05385   else if (hi2c->XferCount == 3U)
05386   {
05387     /* Disable BUF interrupt, this help to treat correctly the last 2 bytes
05388        on BTF subroutine if there is a reception delay between N-1 and N byte */
05389     __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_BUF);
05390 
05391     if ((CurrentXferOptions != I2C_NEXT_FRAME) && (CurrentXferOptions != I2C_FIRST_AND_NEXT_FRAME))
05392     {
05393       /* Disable Acknowledge */
05394       CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
05395     }
05396 
05397     /* Read data from DR */
05398     *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
05399 
05400     /* Increment Buffer pointer */
05401     hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
05402 
05403     /* Update counter */
05404     hi2c->XferCount--;
05405   }
05406   else if (hi2c->XferCount == 2U)
05407   {
05408     /* Prepare next transfer or stop current transfer */
05409     if ((CurrentXferOptions == I2C_FIRST_FRAME) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME_NO_STOP))
05410     {
05411       /* Disable Acknowledge */
05412       CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
05413     }
05414     else if ((CurrentXferOptions == I2C_NEXT_FRAME) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_FIRST_AND_NEXT_FRAME))
05415     {
05416       /* Enable Acknowledge */
05417       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
05418     }
05419     else if (CurrentXferOptions != I2C_LAST_FRAME_NO_STOP)
05420     {
05421       /* Generate Stop */
05422       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
05423     }
05424     else
05425     {
05426       /* Do nothing */
05427     }
05428 
05429     /* Read data from DR */
05430     *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
05431 
05432     /* Increment Buffer pointer */
05433     hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
05434 
05435     /* Update counter */
05436     hi2c->XferCount--;
05437 
05438     /* Read data from DR */
05439     *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
05440 
05441     /* Increment Buffer pointer */
05442     hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
05443 
05444     /* Update counter */
05445     hi2c->XferCount--;
05446 
05447     /* Disable EVT and ERR interrupt */
05448     __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_ERR);
05449 
05450     hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
05451     if (hi2c->Mode == HAL_I2C_MODE_MEM)
05452     {
05453       hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
05454       hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_NONE;
05455 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
05456       hi2c->MemRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05457 #else
05458       HAL_I2C_MemRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05459 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
05460     }
05461     else
05462     {
05463       hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
05464       hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_MASTER_BUSY_RX;
05465 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
05466       hi2c->MasterRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05467 #else
05468       HAL_I2C_MasterRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05469 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
05470     }
05471   }
05472   else
05473   {
05474     /* Read data from DR */
05475     *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
05476 
05477     /* Increment Buffer pointer */
05478     hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
05479 
05480     /* Update counter */
05481     hi2c->XferCount--;
05482   }
05483 }
05484 
05485 /**
05486   * @brief  Handle SB flag for Master
05487   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
05488   *         the configuration information for I2C module
05489   * @retval None
05490   */
05491 static void I2C_Master_SB(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
05492 {
05493   if (hi2c->Mode == HAL_I2C_MODE_MEM)
05494   {
05495     if (hi2c->EventCount == 0U)
05496     {
05497       /* Send slave address */
05498       hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_7BIT_ADD_WRITE(hi2c->Devaddress);
05499     }
05500     else
05501     {
05502       hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_7BIT_ADD_READ(hi2c->Devaddress);
05503     }
05504   }
05505   else
05506   {
05507     if (hi2c->Init.AddressingMode == I2C_ADDRESSINGMODE_7BIT)
05508     {
05509       /* Send slave 7 Bits address */
05510       if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX)
05511       {
05512         hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_7BIT_ADD_WRITE(hi2c->Devaddress);
05513       }
05514       else
05515       {
05516         hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_7BIT_ADD_READ(hi2c->Devaddress);
05517       }
05518 
05519       if ((hi2c->hdmatx != NULL) || (hi2c->hdmarx != NULL))
05520       {
05521         if ((hi2c->hdmatx->XferCpltCallback != NULL) || (hi2c->hdmarx->XferCpltCallback != NULL))
05522         {
05523           /* Enable DMA Request */
05524           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN);
05525         }
05526       }
05527     }
05528     else
05529     {
05530       if (hi2c->EventCount == 0U)
05531       {
05532         /* Send header of slave address */
05533         hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_10BIT_HEADER_WRITE(hi2c->Devaddress);
05534       }
05535       else if (hi2c->EventCount == 1U)
05536       {
05537         /* Send header of slave address */
05538         hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_10BIT_HEADER_READ(hi2c->Devaddress);
05539       }
05540       else
05541       {
05542         /* Do nothing */
05543       }
05544     }
05545   }
05546 }
05547 
05548 /**
05549   * @brief  Handle ADD10 flag for Master
05550   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
05551   *         the configuration information for I2C module
05552   * @retval None
05553   */
05554 static void I2C_Master_ADD10(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
05555 {
05556   /* Send slave address */
05557   hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_10BIT_ADDRESS(hi2c->Devaddress);
05558 
05559   if ((hi2c->hdmatx != NULL) || (hi2c->hdmarx != NULL))
05560   {
05561     if ((hi2c->hdmatx->XferCpltCallback != NULL) || (hi2c->hdmarx->XferCpltCallback != NULL))
05562     {
05563       /* Enable DMA Request */
05564       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN);
05565     }
05566   }
05567 }
05568 
05569 /**
05570   * @brief  Handle ADDR flag for Master
05571   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
05572   *         the configuration information for I2C module
05573   * @retval None
05574   */
05575 static void I2C_Master_ADDR(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
05576 {
05577   /* Declaration of temporary variable to prevent undefined behavior of volatile usage */
05578   HAL_I2C_ModeTypeDef CurrentMode       = hi2c->Mode;
05579   uint32_t CurrentXferOptions           = hi2c->XferOptions;
05580   uint32_t Prev_State                   = hi2c->PreviousState;
05581 
05582   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX)
05583   {
05584     if ((hi2c->EventCount == 0U) && (CurrentMode == HAL_I2C_MODE_MEM))
05585     {
05586       /* Clear ADDR flag */
05587       __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
05588     }
05589     else if ((hi2c->EventCount == 0U) && (hi2c->Init.AddressingMode == I2C_ADDRESSINGMODE_10BIT))
05590     {
05591       /* Clear ADDR flag */
05592       __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
05593 
05594       /* Generate Restart */
05595       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
05596 
05597       hi2c->EventCount++;
05598     }
05599     else
05600     {
05601       if (hi2c->XferCount == 0U)
05602       {
05603         /* Clear ADDR flag */
05604         __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
05605 
05606         /* Generate Stop */
05607         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
05608       }
05609       else if (hi2c->XferCount == 1U)
05610       {
05611         if (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME)
05612         {
05613           /* Disable Acknowledge */
05614           CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
05615 
05616           if ((hi2c->Instance->CR2 & I2C_CR2_DMAEN) == I2C_CR2_DMAEN)
05617           {
05618             /* Disable Acknowledge */
05619             CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
05620 
05621             /* Clear ADDR flag */
05622             __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
05623           }
05624           else
05625           {
05626             /* Clear ADDR flag */
05627             __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
05628 
05629             /* Generate Stop */
05630             SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
05631           }
05632         }
05633         /* Prepare next transfer or stop current transfer */
05634         else if ((CurrentXferOptions != I2C_FIRST_AND_LAST_FRAME) && (CurrentXferOptions != I2C_LAST_FRAME) \
05635                  && ((Prev_State != I2C_STATE_MASTER_BUSY_RX) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_FIRST_FRAME)))
05636         {
05637           if ((CurrentXferOptions != I2C_NEXT_FRAME) && (CurrentXferOptions != I2C_FIRST_AND_NEXT_FRAME) && (CurrentXferOptions != I2C_LAST_FRAME_NO_STOP))
05638           {
05639             /* Disable Acknowledge */
05640             CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
05641           }
05642           else
05643           {
05644             /* Enable Acknowledge */
05645             SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
05646           }
05647 
05648           /* Clear ADDR flag */
05649           __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
05650         }
05651         else
05652         {
05653           /* Disable Acknowledge */
05654           CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
05655 
05656           /* Clear ADDR flag */
05657           __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
05658 
05659           /* Generate Stop */
05660           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
05661         }
05662       }
05663       else if (hi2c->XferCount == 2U)
05664       {
05665         if ((CurrentXferOptions != I2C_NEXT_FRAME) && (CurrentXferOptions != I2C_FIRST_AND_NEXT_FRAME) && (CurrentXferOptions != I2C_LAST_FRAME_NO_STOP))
05666         {
05667           /* Enable Pos */
05668           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_POS);
05669 
05670           /* Clear ADDR flag */
05671           __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
05672 
05673           /* Disable Acknowledge */
05674           CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
05675         }
05676         else
05677         {
05678           /* Enable Acknowledge */
05679           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
05680 
05681           /* Clear ADDR flag */
05682           __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
05683         }
05684 
05685         if (((hi2c->Instance->CR2 & I2C_CR2_DMAEN) == I2C_CR2_DMAEN) && ((CurrentXferOptions == I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_FIRST_FRAME) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_FIRST_AND_LAST_FRAME) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME_NO_STOP) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME)))
05686         {
05687           /* Enable Last DMA bit */
05688           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_LAST);
05689         }
05690       }
05691       else
05692       {
05693         /* Enable Acknowledge */
05694         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
05695 
05696         if (((hi2c->Instance->CR2 & I2C_CR2_DMAEN) == I2C_CR2_DMAEN) && ((CurrentXferOptions == I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_FIRST_FRAME) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_FIRST_AND_LAST_FRAME) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME_NO_STOP) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME)))
05697         {
05698           /* Enable Last DMA bit */
05699           SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_LAST);
05700         }
05701 
05702         /* Clear ADDR flag */
05703         __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
05704       }
05705 
05706       /* Reset Event counter  */
05707       hi2c->EventCount = 0U;
05708     }
05709   }
05710   else
05711   {
05712     /* Clear ADDR flag */
05713     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
05714   }
05715 }
05716 
05717 /**
05718   * @brief  Handle TXE flag for Slave
05719   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
05720   *         the configuration information for I2C module
05721   * @retval None
05722   */
05723 static void I2C_SlaveTransmit_TXE(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
05724 {
05725   /* Declaration of temporary variables to prevent undefined behavior of volatile usage */
05726   HAL_I2C_StateTypeDef CurrentState = hi2c->State;
05727 
05728   if (hi2c->XferCount != 0U)
05729   {
05730     /* Write data to DR */
05731     hi2c->Instance->DR = *hi2c->pBuffPtr;
05732 
05733     /* Increment Buffer pointer */
05734     hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
05735 
05736     /* Update counter */
05737     hi2c->XferCount--;
05738 
05739     if ((hi2c->XferCount == 0U) && (CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX_LISTEN))
05740     {
05741       /* Last Byte is received, disable Interrupt */
05742       __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_BUF);
05743 
05744       /* Set state at HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN */
05745       hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_SLAVE_BUSY_TX;
05746       hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN;
05747 
05748       /* Call the corresponding callback to inform upper layer of End of Transfer */
05749 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
05750       hi2c->SlaveTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05751 #else
05752       HAL_I2C_SlaveTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05753 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
05754     }
05755   }
05756 }
05757

05759   * @brief  Handle BTF flag for Slave transmitter
05760   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
05761   *         the configuration information for I2C module
05762   * @retval None
05763   */
05764 static void I2C_SlaveTransmit_BTF(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)

05768     /* Write data to DR */
05769     hi2c->Instance->DR = *hi2c->pBuffPtr;
05770 
05771     /* Increment Buffer pointer */
05772     hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
05773 
05774     /* Update counter */
05775     hi2c->XferCount--;
05776   }
05777 }

05784   */
05785 static void I2C_SlaveReceive_RXNE(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)

05794 
05795     /* Increment Buffer pointer */
05796     hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
05797 
05798     /* Update counter */
05799     hi2c->XferCount--;
05800 
05801     if ((hi2c->XferCount == 0U) && (CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX_LISTEN))

05809 
05810       /* Call the corresponding callback to inform upper layer of End of Transfer */
05811 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
05812       hi2c->SlaveRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05813 #else
05814       HAL_I2C_SlaveRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
05815 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
05816     }
05817   }

05841 /**
05842   * @brief  Handle ADD flag for Slave
05843   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
05844   *         the configuration information for I2C module
05845   * @param  IT2Flags Interrupt2 flags to handle.
05846   * @retval None
05847   */
05848 static void I2C_Slave_ADDR(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint32_t IT2Flags)
05849 {
05850   uint8_t TransferDirection = I2C_DIRECTION_RECEIVE;
05851   uint16_t SlaveAddrCode;
05852 
05853   if (((uint32_t)hi2c->State & (uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN) == (uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN)
05854   {
05855     /* Disable BUF interrupt, BUF enabling is manage through slave specific interface */
05856     __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, (I2C_IT_BUF));
05857 
05858     /* Transfer Direction requested by Master */
05859     if (I2C_CHECK_FLAG(IT2Flags, I2C_FLAG_TRA) == RESET)
05860     {
05861       TransferDirection = I2C_DIRECTION_TRANSMIT;
05862     }
05863 
05864     if (I2C_CHECK_FLAG(IT2Flags, I2C_FLAG_DUALF) == RESET)
05865     {
05866       SlaveAddrCode = (uint16_t)hi2c->Init.OwnAddress1;
05867     }
05868     else
05869     {
05870       SlaveAddrCode = (uint16_t)hi2c->Init.OwnAddress2;
05871     }
05872 
05873     /* Process Unlocked */
05874     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
05875 
05876     /* Call Slave Addr callback */
05877 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
05878     hi2c->AddrCallback(hi2c, TransferDirection, SlaveAddrCode);
05879 #else
05880     HAL_I2C_AddrCallback(hi2c, TransferDirection, SlaveAddrCode);
05881 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
05882   }
05883   else
05884   {
05885     /* Clear ADDR flag */
05886     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_ADDR);
05887 
05888     /* Process Unlocked */
05889     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
05890   }
05891 }
05892 
05893 /**
05894   * @brief  Handle STOPF flag for Slave
05895   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
05896   *         the configuration information for I2C module
05897   * @retval None
05898   */
05899 static void I2C_Slave_STOPF(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
05900 {
05901   /* Declaration of temporary variable to prevent undefined behavior of volatile usage */
05902   HAL_I2C_StateTypeDef CurrentState = hi2c->State;
05903 
05904   /* Disable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
05905   __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
05906 
05907   /* Clear STOPF flag */
05908   __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_STOPFLAG(hi2c);
05909 
05910   /* Disable Acknowledge */
05911   CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
05912 
05913   /* If a DMA is ongoing, Update handle size context */
05914   if ((hi2c->Instance->CR2 & I2C_CR2_DMAEN) == I2C_CR2_DMAEN)
05915   {
05916     if ((CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX) || (CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX_LISTEN))
05917     {
05918       hi2c->XferCount = (uint16_t)(__HAL_DMA_GET_COUNTER(hi2c->hdmarx));
05919 
05920       if (hi2c->XferCount != 0U)
05921       {
05922         /* Set ErrorCode corresponding to a Non-Acknowledge */
05923         hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF;
05924       }
05925 
05926       /* Disable, stop the current DMA */
05927       CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN);
05928 
05929       /* Abort DMA Xfer if any */
05930       if (HAL_DMA_GetState(hi2c->hdmarx) != HAL_DMA_STATE_READY)
05931       {
05932         /* Set the I2C DMA Abort callback :
05933         will lead to call HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback() at end of DMA abort procedure */
05934         hi2c->hdmarx->XferAbortCallback = I2C_DMAAbort;
05935 
05936         /* Abort DMA RX */
05937         if (HAL_DMA_Abort_IT(hi2c->hdmarx) != HAL_OK)
05938         {
05939           /* Call Directly XferAbortCallback function in case of error */
05940           hi2c->hdmarx->XferAbortCallback(hi2c->hdmarx);
05941         }
05942       }
05943     }
05944     else
05945     {
05946       hi2c->XferCount = (uint16_t)(__HAL_DMA_GET_COUNTER(hi2c->hdmatx));
05947 
05948       if (hi2c->XferCount != 0U)
05949       {
05950         /* Set ErrorCode corresponding to a Non-Acknowledge */
05951         hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF;
05952       }
05953 
05954       /* Disable, stop the current DMA */
05955       CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN);
05956 
05957       /* Abort DMA Xfer if any */
05958       if (HAL_DMA_GetState(hi2c->hdmatx) != HAL_DMA_STATE_READY)
05959       {
05960         /* Set the I2C DMA Abort callback :
05961         will lead to call HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback() at end of DMA abort procedure */
05962         hi2c->hdmatx->XferAbortCallback = I2C_DMAAbort;
05963 
05964         /* Abort DMA TX */
05965         if (HAL_DMA_Abort_IT(hi2c->hdmatx) != HAL_OK)
05966         {
05967           /* Call Directly XferAbortCallback function in case of error */
05968           hi2c->hdmatx->XferAbortCallback(hi2c->hdmatx);
05969         }
05970       }
05971     }
05972   }
05973 
05974   /* All data are not transferred, so set error code accordingly */
05975   if (hi2c->XferCount != 0U)
05976   {
05977     /* Store Last receive data if any */
05978     if (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_BTF) == SET)
05979     {
05980       /* Read data from DR */
05981       *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
05982 
05983       /* Increment Buffer pointer */
05984       hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
05985 
05986       /* Update counter */
05987       hi2c->XferCount--;
05988     }
05989 
05990     /* Store Last receive data if any */
05991     if (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_RXNE) == SET)
05992     {
05993       /* Read data from DR */
05994       *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
05995 
05996       /* Increment Buffer pointer */
05997       hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
05998 
05999       /* Update counter */
06000       hi2c->XferCount--;
06001     }
06002 
06003     if (hi2c->XferCount != 0U)
06004     {
06005       /* Set ErrorCode corresponding to a Non-Acknowledge */
06006       hi2c->ErrorCode |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF;
06007     }
06008   }
06009 
06010   if (hi2c->ErrorCode != HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE)
06011   {
06012     /* Call the corresponding callback to inform upper layer of End of Transfer */
06013     I2C_ITError(hi2c);
06014   }
06015   else
06016   {
06017     if (CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX_LISTEN)
06018     {
06019       /* Set state at HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN */
06020       hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_NONE;
06021       hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN;
06022 
06023       /* Call the corresponding callback to inform upper layer of End of Transfer */
06024 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
06025       hi2c->SlaveRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
06026 #else
06027       HAL_I2C_SlaveRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
06028 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
06029     }
06030 
06031     if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN)
06032     {
06033       hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
06034       hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_NONE;
06035       hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06036       hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
06037 
06038       /* Call the Listen Complete callback, to inform upper layer of the end of Listen usecase */
06039 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
06040       hi2c->ListenCpltCallback(hi2c);
06041 #else
06042       HAL_I2C_ListenCpltCallback(hi2c);
06043 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
06044     }
06045     else
06046     {
06047       if ((hi2c->PreviousState  == I2C_STATE_SLAVE_BUSY_RX) || (CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX))
06048       {
06049         hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_NONE;
06050         hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06051         hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
06052 
06053 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
06054         hi2c->SlaveRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
06055 #else
06056         HAL_I2C_SlaveRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
06057 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
06058       }
06059     }
06060   }
06061 }
06062 
06063 /**
06064   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
06065   *         the configuration information for I2C module
06066   * @retval None
06067   */
06068 static void I2C_Slave_AF(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
06069 {
06070   /* Declaration of temporary variables to prevent undefined behavior of volatile usage */
06071   HAL_I2C_StateTypeDef CurrentState = hi2c->State;
06072   uint32_t CurrentXferOptions       = hi2c->XferOptions;
06073 
06074   if (((CurrentXferOptions ==  I2C_FIRST_AND_LAST_FRAME) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME)) && \
06075       (CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN))
06076   {
06077     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
06078 
06079     /* Disable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
06080     __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
06081 
06082     /* Clear AF flag */
06083     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_AF);
06084 
06085     /* Disable Acknowledge */
06086     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
06087 
06088     hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_NONE;
06089     hi2c->State         = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06090     hi2c->Mode          = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
06091 
06092     /* Call the Listen Complete callback, to inform upper layer of the end of Listen usecase */
06093 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
06094     hi2c->ListenCpltCallback(hi2c);
06095 #else
06096     HAL_I2C_ListenCpltCallback(hi2c);
06097 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
06098   }
06099   else if (CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX)
06100   {
06101     hi2c->XferOptions   = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
06102     hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_SLAVE_BUSY_TX;
06103     hi2c->State         = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06104     hi2c->Mode          = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
06105 
06106     /* Disable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
06107     __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
06108 
06109     /* Clear AF flag */
06110     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_AF);
06111 
06112     /* Disable Acknowledge */
06113     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
06114 
06115 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
06116     hi2c->SlaveTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
06117 #else
06118     HAL_I2C_SlaveTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
06119 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
06120   }
06121   else
06122   {
06123     /* Clear AF flag only */
06124     /* State Listen, but XferOptions == FIRST or NEXT */
06125     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_AF);
06126   }
06127 }
06128 
06129 /**
06130   * @brief  I2C interrupts error process
06131   * @param  hi2c I2C handle.
06132   * @retval None
06133   */
06134 static void I2C_ITError(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
06135 {
06136   /* Declaration of temporary variable to prevent undefined behavior of volatile usage */
06137   HAL_I2C_StateTypeDef CurrentState = hi2c->State;
06138 
06139   if ((hi2c->Mode == HAL_I2C_MODE_MASTER) && (CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX))
06140   {
06141     /* Disable Pos bit in I2C CR1 when error occurred in Master/Mem Receive IT Process */
06142     hi2c->Instance->CR1 &= ~I2C_CR1_POS;
06143   }
06144 
06145   if (((uint32_t)CurrentState & (uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN) == (uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN)
06146   {
06147     /* keep HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN */
06148     hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_NONE;
06149     hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN;
06150   }
06151   else
06152   {
06153     /* If state is an abort treatment on going, don't change state */
06154     /* This change will be do later */
06155     if ((READ_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN) != I2C_CR2_DMAEN) && (CurrentState != HAL_I2C_STATE_ABORT))
06156     {
06157       hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06158     }
06159     hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_NONE;
06160     hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
06161   }
06162 
06163   /* Abort DMA transfer */
06164   if (READ_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN) == I2C_CR2_DMAEN)
06165   {
06166     hi2c->Instance->CR2 &= ~I2C_CR2_DMAEN;
06167 
06168     if (hi2c->hdmatx->State != HAL_DMA_STATE_READY)
06169     {
06170       /* Set the DMA Abort callback :
06171       will lead to call HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback() at end of DMA abort procedure */
06172       hi2c->hdmatx->XferAbortCallback = I2C_DMAAbort;
06173 
06174       if (HAL_DMA_Abort_IT(hi2c->hdmatx) != HAL_OK)
06175       {
06176         /* Disable I2C peripheral to prevent dummy data in buffer */
06177         __HAL_I2C_DISABLE(hi2c);
06178 
06179         hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06180 
06181         /* Call Directly XferAbortCallback function in case of error */
06182         hi2c->hdmatx->XferAbortCallback(hi2c->hdmatx);
06183       }
06184     }
06185     else
06186     {
06187       /* Set the DMA Abort callback :
06188       will lead to call HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback() at end of DMA abort procedure */
06189       hi2c->hdmarx->XferAbortCallback = I2C_DMAAbort;
06190 
06191       if (HAL_DMA_Abort_IT(hi2c->hdmarx) != HAL_OK)
06192       {
06193         /* Store Last receive data if any */
06194         if (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_RXNE) == SET)
06195         {
06196           /* Read data from DR */
06197           *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
06198 
06199           /* Increment Buffer pointer */
06200           hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
06201         }
06202 
06203         /* Disable I2C peripheral to prevent dummy data in buffer */
06204         __HAL_I2C_DISABLE(hi2c);
06205 
06206         hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06207 
06208         /* Call Directly hi2c->hdmarx->XferAbortCallback function in case of error */
06209         hi2c->hdmarx->XferAbortCallback(hi2c->hdmarx);
06210       }
06211     }
06212   }
06213   else if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_ABORT)
06214   {
06215     hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06216     hi2c->ErrorCode = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
06217 
06218     /* Store Last receive data if any */
06219     if (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_RXNE) == SET)
06220     {
06221       /* Read data from DR */
06222       *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
06223 
06224       /* Increment Buffer pointer */
06225       hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
06226     }
06227 
06228     /* Disable I2C peripheral to prevent dummy data in buffer */
06229     __HAL_I2C_DISABLE(hi2c);
06230 
06231     /* Call the corresponding callback to inform upper layer of End of Transfer */
06232 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
06233     hi2c->AbortCpltCallback(hi2c);
06234 #else
06235     HAL_I2C_AbortCpltCallback(hi2c);
06236 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
06237   }
06238   else
06239   {
06240     /* Store Last receive data if any */
06241     if (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_RXNE) == SET)
06242     {
06243       /* Read data from DR */
06244       *hi2c->pBuffPtr = (uint8_t)hi2c->Instance->DR;
06245 
06246       /* Increment Buffer pointer */
06247       hi2c->pBuffPtr++;
06248     }
06249 
06250     /* Call user error callback */
06251 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
06252     hi2c->ErrorCallback(hi2c);
06253 #else
06254     HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback(hi2c);
06255 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
06256   }
06257   /* STOP Flag is not set after a NACK reception */
06258   /* So may inform upper layer that listen phase is stopped */
06259   /* during NACK error treatment */
06260   CurrentState = hi2c->State;
06261   if (((hi2c->ErrorCode & HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF) == HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF) && (CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN))
06262   {
06263     /* Disable EVT, BUF and ERR interrupt */
06264     __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_BUF | I2C_IT_ERR);
06265 
06266     hi2c->XferOptions   = I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME;
06267     hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_NONE;
06268     hi2c->State         = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06269     hi2c->Mode          = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
06270 
06271     /* Call the Listen Complete callback, to inform upper layer of the end of Listen usecase */
06272 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
06273     hi2c->ListenCpltCallback(hi2c);
06274 #else
06275     HAL_I2C_ListenCpltCallback(hi2c);
06276 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
06277   }
06278 }
06279 
06280 /**
06281   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
06282   *         the configuration information for I2C module
06283   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
06284   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
06285   * @param  Timeout Timeout duration
06286   * @param  Tickstart Tick start value
06287   * @retval HAL status
06288   */
06289 static HAL_StatusTypeDef I2C_MasterRequestWrite(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint32_t Timeout, uint32_t Tickstart)
06290 {
06291   /* Declaration of temporary variable to prevent undefined behavior of volatile usage */
06292   uint32_t CurrentXferOptions = hi2c->XferOptions;
06293 
06294   /* Generate Start condition if first transfer */
06295   if ((CurrentXferOptions == I2C_FIRST_AND_LAST_FRAME) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_FIRST_FRAME) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME))
06296   {
06297     /* Generate Start */
06298     SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
06299   }
06300   else if (hi2c->PreviousState == I2C_STATE_MASTER_BUSY_RX)
06301   {
06302     /* Generate ReStart */
06303     SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
06304   }
06305   else
06306   {
06307     /* Do nothing */
06308   }
06309 
06310   /* Wait until SB flag is set */
06311   if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_SB, RESET, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06312   {
06313     return HAL_ERROR;
06314   }
06315 
06316   if (hi2c->Init.AddressingMode == I2C_ADDRESSINGMODE_7BIT)
06317   {
06318     /* Send slave address */
06319     hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_7BIT_ADD_WRITE(DevAddress);
06320   }
06321   else
06322   {
06323     /* Send header of slave address */
06324     hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_10BIT_HEADER_WRITE(DevAddress);
06325 
06326     /* Wait until ADD10 flag is set */
06327     if (I2C_WaitOnMasterAddressFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_ADD10, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06328     {
06329       return HAL_ERROR;
06330     }
06331 
06332     /* Send slave address */
06333     hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_10BIT_ADDRESS(DevAddress);
06334   }
06335 
06336   /* Wait until ADDR flag is set */
06337   if (I2C_WaitOnMasterAddressFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_ADDR, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06338   {
06339     return HAL_ERROR;
06340   }
06341 
06342   return HAL_OK;
06343 }
06344 
06345 /**
06346   * @brief  Master sends target device address for read request.
06347   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
06348   *         the configuration information for I2C module
06349   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
06350   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
06351   * @param  Timeout Timeout duration
06352   * @param  Tickstart Tick start value
06353   * @retval HAL status
06354   */
06355 static HAL_StatusTypeDef I2C_MasterRequestRead(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint32_t Timeout, uint32_t Tickstart)
06356 {
06357   /* Declaration of temporary variable to prevent undefined behavior of volatile usage */
06358   uint32_t CurrentXferOptions = hi2c->XferOptions;
06359 
06360   /* Enable Acknowledge */
06361   SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
06362 
06363   /* Generate Start condition if first transfer */
06364   if ((CurrentXferOptions == I2C_FIRST_AND_LAST_FRAME) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_FIRST_FRAME)  || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME))
06365   {
06366     /* Generate Start */
06367     SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
06368   }
06369   else if (hi2c->PreviousState == I2C_STATE_MASTER_BUSY_TX)
06370   {
06371     /* Generate ReStart */
06372     SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
06373   }
06374   else
06375   {
06376     /* Do nothing */
06377   }
06378 
06379   /* Wait until SB flag is set */
06380   if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_SB, RESET, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06381   {
06382     return HAL_ERROR;
06383   }
06384 
06385   if (hi2c->Init.AddressingMode == I2C_ADDRESSINGMODE_7BIT)
06386   {
06387     /* Send slave address */
06388     hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_7BIT_ADD_READ(DevAddress);
06389   }
06390   else
06391   {
06392     /* Send header of slave address */
06393     hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_10BIT_HEADER_WRITE(DevAddress);
06394 
06395     /* Wait until ADD10 flag is set */
06396     if (I2C_WaitOnMasterAddressFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_ADD10, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06397     {
06398       return HAL_ERROR;
06399     }
06400 
06401     /* Send slave address */
06402     hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_10BIT_ADDRESS(DevAddress);
06403 
06404     /* Wait until ADDR flag is set */
06405     if (I2C_WaitOnMasterAddressFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_ADDR, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06406     {
06407       return HAL_ERROR;
06408     }
06409 
06410     /* Clear ADDR flag */
06411     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
06412 
06413     /* Generate Restart */
06414     SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
06415 
06416     /* Wait until SB flag is set */
06417     if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_SB, RESET, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06418     {
06419       return HAL_ERROR;
06420     }
06421 
06422     /* Send header of slave address */
06423     hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_10BIT_HEADER_READ(DevAddress);
06424   }
06425 
06426   /* Wait until ADDR flag is set */
06427   if (I2C_WaitOnMasterAddressFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_ADDR, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06428   {
06429     return HAL_ERROR;
06430   }
06431 
06432   return HAL_OK;
06433 }
06434 
06435 /**
06436   * @brief  Master sends target device address followed by internal memory address for write request.
06437   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
06438   *         the configuration information for I2C module
06439   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
06440   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
06441   * @param  MemAddress Internal memory address
06442   * @param  MemAddSize Size of internal memory address
06443   * @param  Timeout Timeout duration
06444   * @param  Tickstart Tick start value
06445   * @retval HAL status
06446   */
06447 static HAL_StatusTypeDef I2C_RequestMemoryWrite(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint16_t MemAddress, uint16_t MemAddSize, uint32_t Timeout, uint32_t Tickstart)
06448 {
06449   /* Generate Start */
06450   SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
06451 
06452   /* Wait until SB flag is set */
06453   if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_SB, RESET, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06454   {
06455     return HAL_ERROR;
06456   }
06457 
06458   /* Send slave address */
06459   hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_7BIT_ADD_WRITE(DevAddress);
06460 
06461   /* Wait until ADDR flag is set */
06462   if (I2C_WaitOnMasterAddressFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_ADDR, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06463   {
06464     return HAL_ERROR;
06465   }
06466 
06467   /* Clear ADDR flag */
06468   __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
06469 
06470   /* Wait until TXE flag is set */
06471   if (I2C_WaitOnTXEFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06472   {
06473     if (hi2c->ErrorCode == HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF)
06474     {
06475       /* Generate Stop */
06476       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
06477     }
06478     return HAL_ERROR;
06479   }
06480 
06481   /* If Memory address size is 8Bit */
06482   if (MemAddSize == I2C_MEMADD_SIZE_8BIT)
06483   {
06484     /* Send Memory Address */
06485     hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_MEM_ADD_LSB(MemAddress);
06486   }
06487   /* If Memory address size is 16Bit */
06488   else
06489   {
06490     /* Send MSB of Memory Address */
06491     hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_MEM_ADD_MSB(MemAddress);
06492 
06493     /* Wait until TXE flag is set */
06494     if (I2C_WaitOnTXEFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06495     {
06496       if (hi2c->ErrorCode == HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF)
06497       {
06498         /* Generate Stop */
06499         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
06500       }
06501       return HAL_ERROR;
06502     }
06503 
06504     /* Send LSB of Memory Address */
06505     hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_MEM_ADD_LSB(MemAddress);
06506   }
06507 
06508   return HAL_OK;
06509 }
06510 
06511 /**
06512   * @brief  Master sends target device address followed by internal memory address for read request.
06513   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
06514   *         the configuration information for I2C module
06515   * @param  DevAddress Target device address: The device 7 bits address value
06516   *         in datasheet must be shifted to the left before calling the interface
06517   * @param  MemAddress Internal memory address
06518   * @param  MemAddSize Size of internal memory address
06519   * @param  Timeout Timeout duration
06520   * @param  Tickstart Tick start value
06521   * @retval HAL status
06522   */
06523 static HAL_StatusTypeDef I2C_RequestMemoryRead(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint16_t DevAddress, uint16_t MemAddress, uint16_t MemAddSize, uint32_t Timeout, uint32_t Tickstart)
06524 {
06525   /* Enable Acknowledge */
06526   SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
06527 
06528   /* Generate Start */
06529   SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
06530 
06531   /* Wait until SB flag is set */
06532   if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_SB, RESET, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06533   {
06534     return HAL_ERROR;
06535   }
06536 
06537   /* Send slave address */
06538   hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_7BIT_ADD_WRITE(DevAddress);
06539 
06540   /* Wait until ADDR flag is set */
06541   if (I2C_WaitOnMasterAddressFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_ADDR, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06542   {
06543     return HAL_ERROR;
06544   }
06545 
06546   /* Clear ADDR flag */
06547   __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_ADDRFLAG(hi2c);
06548 
06549   /* Wait until TXE flag is set */
06550   if (I2C_WaitOnTXEFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06551   {
06552     if (hi2c->ErrorCode == HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF)
06553     {
06554       /* Generate Stop */
06555       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
06556     }
06557     return HAL_ERROR;
06558   }
06559 
06560   /* If Memory address size is 8Bit */
06561   if (MemAddSize == I2C_MEMADD_SIZE_8BIT)
06562   {
06563     /* Send Memory Address */
06564     hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_MEM_ADD_LSB(MemAddress);
06565   }
06566   /* If Memory address size is 16Bit */
06567   else
06568   {
06569     /* Send MSB of Memory Address */
06570     hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_MEM_ADD_MSB(MemAddress);
06571 
06572     /* Wait until TXE flag is set */
06573     if (I2C_WaitOnTXEFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06574     {
06575       if (hi2c->ErrorCode == HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF)
06576       {
06577         /* Generate Stop */
06578         SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
06579       }
06580       return HAL_ERROR;
06581     }
06582 
06583     /* Send LSB of Memory Address */
06584     hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_MEM_ADD_LSB(MemAddress);
06585   }
06586 
06587   /* Wait until TXE flag is set */
06588   if (I2C_WaitOnTXEFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06589   {
06590     if (hi2c->ErrorCode == HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF)
06591     {
06592       /* Generate Stop */
06593       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
06594     }
06595     return HAL_ERROR;
06596   }
06597 
06598   /* Generate Restart */
06599   SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_START);
06600 
06601   /* Wait until SB flag is set */
06602   if (I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_SB, RESET, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06603   {
06604     return HAL_ERROR;
06605   }
06606 
06607   /* Send slave address */
06608   hi2c->Instance->DR = I2C_7BIT_ADD_READ(DevAddress);
06609 
06610   /* Wait until ADDR flag is set */
06611   if (I2C_WaitOnMasterAddressFlagUntilTimeout(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_ADDR, Timeout, Tickstart) != HAL_OK)
06612   {
06613     return HAL_ERROR;
06614   }
06615 
06616   return HAL_OK;
06617 }
06618 
06619 /**
06620   * @brief  DMA I2C process complete callback.
06621   * @param  hdma DMA handle
06622   * @retval None
06623   */
06624 static void I2C_DMAXferCplt(DMA_HandleTypeDef *hdma)
06625 {
06626   I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c = (I2C_HandleTypeDef *)((DMA_HandleTypeDef *)hdma)->Parent; /* Derogation MISRAC2012-Rule-11.5 */
06627 
06628   /* Declaration of temporary variable to prevent undefined behavior of volatile usage */
06629   HAL_I2C_StateTypeDef CurrentState = hi2c->State;
06630   HAL_I2C_ModeTypeDef CurrentMode   = hi2c->Mode;
06631   uint32_t CurrentXferOptions       = hi2c->XferOptions;
06632 
06633   /* Disable EVT and ERR interrupt */
06634   __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_ERR);
06635 
06636   /* Clear Complete callback */
06637   hi2c->hdmatx->XferCpltCallback = NULL;
06638   hi2c->hdmarx->XferCpltCallback = NULL;
06639 
06640   if ((((uint32_t)CurrentState & (uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX) == (uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX) || ((((uint32_t)CurrentState & (uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX) == (uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX) && (CurrentMode == HAL_I2C_MODE_SLAVE)))
06641   {
06642     /* Disable DMA Request */
06643     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN);
06644 
06645     hi2c->XferCount = 0U;
06646 
06647     if (CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_TX_LISTEN)
06648     {
06649       /* Set state at HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN */
06650       hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_SLAVE_BUSY_TX;
06651       hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN;
06652 
06653       /* Call the corresponding callback to inform upper layer of End of Transfer */
06654 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
06655       hi2c->SlaveTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
06656 #else
06657       HAL_I2C_SlaveTxCpltCallback(hi2c);
06658 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
06659     }
06660     else if (CurrentState == HAL_I2C_STATE_BUSY_RX_LISTEN)
06661     {
06662       /* Set state at HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN */
06663       hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_SLAVE_BUSY_RX;
06664       hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN;
06665 
06666       /* Call the corresponding callback to inform upper layer of End of Transfer */
06667 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
06668       hi2c->SlaveRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
06669 #else
06670       HAL_I2C_SlaveRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
06671 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
06672     }
06673     else
06674     {
06675       /* Do nothing */
06676     }
06677 
06678     /* Enable EVT and ERR interrupt to treat end of transfer in IRQ handler */
06679     __HAL_I2C_ENABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_ERR);
06680   }
06681   /* Check current Mode, in case of treatment DMA handler have been preempted by a prior interrupt */
06682   else if (hi2c->Mode != HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE)
06683   {
06684     if (hi2c->XferCount == (uint16_t)1)
06685     {
06686       /* Disable Acknowledge */
06687       CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
06688     }
06689 
06690     /* Disable EVT and ERR interrupt */
06691     __HAL_I2C_DISABLE_IT(hi2c, I2C_IT_EVT | I2C_IT_ERR);
06692 
06693     /* Prepare next transfer or stop current transfer */
06694     if ((CurrentXferOptions == I2C_NO_OPTION_FRAME) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_FIRST_AND_LAST_FRAME) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_OTHER_AND_LAST_FRAME) || (CurrentXferOptions == I2C_LAST_FRAME))
06695     {
06696       /* Generate Stop */
06697       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
06698     }
06699 
06700     /* Disable Last DMA */
06701     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_LAST);
06702 
06703     /* Disable DMA Request */
06704     CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR2, I2C_CR2_DMAEN);
06705 
06706     hi2c->XferCount = 0U;
06707 
06708     /* Check if Errors has been detected during transfer */
06709     if (hi2c->ErrorCode != HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE)
06710     {
06711 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
06712       hi2c->ErrorCallback(hi2c);
06713 #else
06714       HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback(hi2c);
06715 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
06716     }
06717     else
06718     {
06719       hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06720 
06721       if (hi2c->Mode == HAL_I2C_MODE_MEM)
06722       {
06723         hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
06724         hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_NONE;
06725 
06726 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
06727         hi2c->MemRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
06728 #else
06729         HAL_I2C_MemRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
06730 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
06731       }
06732       else
06733       {
06734         hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
06735         hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_MASTER_BUSY_RX;
06736 
06737 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
06738         hi2c->MasterRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
06739 #else
06740         HAL_I2C_MasterRxCpltCallback(hi2c);
06741 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
06742       }
06743     }
06744   }
06745   else
06746   {
06747     /* Do nothing */
06748   }
06749 }
06750 
06751 /**
06752   * @brief  DMA I2C communication error callback.
06753   * @param  hdma DMA handle
06754   * @retval None
06755   */
06756 static void I2C_DMAError(DMA_HandleTypeDef *hdma)
06757 {
06758   I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c = (I2C_HandleTypeDef *)((DMA_HandleTypeDef *)hdma)->Parent; /* Derogation MISRAC2012-Rule-11.5 */
06759 
06760   /* Clear Complete callback */
06761   hi2c->hdmatx->XferCpltCallback = NULL;
06762   hi2c->hdmarx->XferCpltCallback = NULL;
06763 
06764   /* Disable Acknowledge */
06765   CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
06766 
06767   hi2c->XferCount       = 0U;
06768   hi2c->State           = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06769   hi2c->Mode            = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
06770   hi2c->ErrorCode       |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_DMA;
06771 
06772 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
06773   hi2c->ErrorCallback(hi2c);
06774 #else
06775   HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback(hi2c);
06776 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
06777 }
06778 
06779 /**
06780   * @brief DMA I2C communication abort callback
06781   *        (To be called at end of DMA Abort procedure).
06782   * @param hdma DMA handle.
06783   * @retval None
06784   */
06785 static void I2C_DMAAbort(DMA_HandleTypeDef *hdma)
06786 {
06787   I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c = (I2C_HandleTypeDef *)((DMA_HandleTypeDef *)hdma)->Parent; /* Derogation MISRAC2012-Rule-11.5 */
06788 
06789   /* Declaration of temporary variable to prevent undefined behavior of volatile usage */
06790   HAL_I2C_StateTypeDef CurrentState = hi2c->State;
06791 
06792   /* Clear Complete callback */
06793   hi2c->hdmatx->XferCpltCallback = NULL;
06794   hi2c->hdmarx->XferCpltCallback = NULL;
06795 
06796   /* Disable Acknowledge */
06797   CLEAR_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
06798 
06799   hi2c->XferCount = 0U;
06800 
06801   /* Reset XferAbortCallback */
06802   hi2c->hdmatx->XferAbortCallback = NULL;
06803   hi2c->hdmarx->XferAbortCallback = NULL;
06804 
06805   /* Disable I2C peripheral to prevent dummy data in buffer */
06806   __HAL_I2C_DISABLE(hi2c);
06807 
06808   /* Check if come from abort from user */
06809   if (hi2c->State == HAL_I2C_STATE_ABORT)
06810   {
06811     hi2c->State         = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06812     hi2c->Mode          = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
06813     hi2c->ErrorCode     = HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
06814 
06815     /* Call the corresponding callback to inform upper layer of End of Transfer */
06816 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
06817     hi2c->AbortCpltCallback(hi2c);
06818 #else
06819     HAL_I2C_AbortCpltCallback(hi2c);
06820 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
06821   }
06822   else
06823   {
06824     if (((uint32_t)CurrentState & (uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN) == (uint32_t)HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN)
06825     {
06826       /* Renable I2C peripheral */
06827       __HAL_I2C_ENABLE(hi2c);
06828 
06829       /* Enable Acknowledge */
06830       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_ACK);
06831 
06832       /* keep HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN */
06833       hi2c->PreviousState = I2C_STATE_NONE;
06834       hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_LISTEN;
06835     }
06836     else
06837     {
06838       hi2c->State = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06839       hi2c->Mode = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
06840     }
06841 
06842     /* Call the corresponding callback to inform upper layer of End of Transfer */
06843 #if (USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS == 1)
06844     hi2c->ErrorCallback(hi2c);
06845 #else
06846     HAL_I2C_ErrorCallback(hi2c);
06847 #endif /* USE_HAL_I2C_REGISTER_CALLBACKS */
06848   }
06849 }
06850 
06851 /**
06852   * @brief  This function handles I2C Communication Timeout.
06853   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
06854   *         the configuration information for I2C module
06855   * @param  Flag specifies the I2C flag to check.
06856   * @param  Status The new Flag status (SET or RESET).
06857   * @param  Timeout Timeout duration
06858   * @param  Tickstart Tick start value
06859   * @retval HAL status
06860   */
06861 static HAL_StatusTypeDef I2C_WaitOnFlagUntilTimeout(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint32_t Flag, FlagStatus Status, uint32_t Timeout, uint32_t Tickstart)
06862 {
06863   /* Wait until flag is set */
06864   while (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, Flag) == Status)
06865   {
06866     /* Check for the Timeout */
06867     if (Timeout != HAL_MAX_DELAY)
06868     {
06869       if (((HAL_GetTick() - Tickstart) > Timeout) || (Timeout == 0U))
06870       {
06871         hi2c->PreviousState     = I2C_STATE_NONE;
06872         hi2c->State             = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06873         hi2c->Mode              = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
06874         hi2c->ErrorCode         |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_TIMEOUT;
06875 
06876         /* Process Unlocked */
06877         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
06878 
06879         return HAL_ERROR;
06880       }
06881     }
06882   }
06883   return HAL_OK;
06884 }
06885 
06886 /**
06887   * @brief  This function handles I2C Communication Timeout for Master addressing phase.
06888   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
06889   *         the configuration information for I2C module
06890   * @param  Flag specifies the I2C flag to check.
06891   * @param  Timeout Timeout duration
06892   * @param  Tickstart Tick start value
06893   * @retval HAL status
06894   */
06895 static HAL_StatusTypeDef I2C_WaitOnMasterAddressFlagUntilTimeout(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint32_t Flag, uint32_t Timeout, uint32_t Tickstart)
06896 {
06897   while (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, Flag) == RESET)
06898   {
06899     if (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_AF) == SET)
06900     {
06901       /* Generate Stop */
06902       SET_BIT(hi2c->Instance->CR1, I2C_CR1_STOP);
06903 
06904       /* Clear AF Flag */
06905       __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_AF);
06906 
06907       hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
06908       hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06909       hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
06910       hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF;
06911 
06912       /* Process Unlocked */
06913       __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
06914 
06915       return HAL_ERROR;
06916     }
06917 
06918     /* Check for the Timeout */
06919     if (Timeout != HAL_MAX_DELAY)
06920     {
06921       if (((HAL_GetTick() - Tickstart) > Timeout) || (Timeout == 0U))
06922       {
06923         hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
06924         hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06925         hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
06926         hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_TIMEOUT;
06927 
06928         /* Process Unlocked */
06929         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
06930 
06931         return HAL_ERROR;
06932       }
06933     }
06934   }
06935   return HAL_OK;
06936 }
06937 
06938 /**
06939   * @brief  This function handles I2C Communication Timeout for specific usage of TXE flag.
06940   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
06941   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
06942   * @param  Timeout Timeout duration
06943   * @param  Tickstart Tick start value
06944   * @retval HAL status
06945   */
06946 static HAL_StatusTypeDef I2C_WaitOnTXEFlagUntilTimeout(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint32_t Timeout, uint32_t Tickstart)
06947 {
06948   while (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_TXE) == RESET)
06949   {
06950     /* Check if a NACK is detected */
06951     if (I2C_IsAcknowledgeFailed(hi2c) != HAL_OK)
06952     {
06953       return HAL_ERROR;
06954     }
06955 
06956     /* Check for the Timeout */
06957     if (Timeout != HAL_MAX_DELAY)
06958     {
06959       if (((HAL_GetTick() - Tickstart) > Timeout) || (Timeout == 0U))
06960       {
06961         hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
06962         hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
06963         hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
06964         hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_TIMEOUT;
06965 
06966         /* Process Unlocked */
06967         __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
06968 
06969         return HAL_ERROR;
06970       }
06971     }
06972   }
06973   return HAL_OK;
06974 }
06975

07050   * @brief  This function handles I2C Communication Timeout for specific usage of RXNE flag.
07051   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
07052   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
07053   * @param  Timeout Timeout duration
07054   * @param  Tickstart Tick start value
07055   * @retval HAL status
07056   */
07057 static HAL_StatusTypeDef I2C_WaitOnRXNEFlagUntilTimeout(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c, uint32_t Timeout, uint32_t Tickstart)
07058 {
07059 
07060   while (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_RXNE) == RESET)

07064     {
07065       /* Clear STOP Flag */
07066       __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_STOPF);
07067 
07068       hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
07069       hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
07070       hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
07071       hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_NONE;
07072 
07073       /* Process Unlocked */
07074       __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
07075 
07076       return HAL_ERROR;
07077     }
07078 
07079     /* Check for the Timeout */
07080     if (((HAL_GetTick() - Tickstart) > Timeout) || (Timeout == 0U))
07081     {
07082       hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
07083       hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
07084       hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
07085       hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_TIMEOUT;
07086 
07087       /* Process Unlocked */
07088       __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
07089 
07090       return HAL_ERROR;
07091     }
07092   }
07093   return HAL_OK;
07094 }

07096 /**
07097   * @brief  This function handles Acknowledge failed detection during an I2C Communication.
07098   * @param  hi2c Pointer to a I2C_HandleTypeDef structure that contains
07099   *                the configuration information for the specified I2C.
07100   * @retval HAL status
07101   */
07102 static HAL_StatusTypeDef I2C_IsAcknowledgeFailed(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
07103 {
07104   if (__HAL_I2C_GET_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_AF) == SET)
07105   {
07106     /* Clear NACKF Flag */
07107     __HAL_I2C_CLEAR_FLAG(hi2c, I2C_FLAG_AF);
07108 
07109     hi2c->PreviousState       = I2C_STATE_NONE;
07110     hi2c->State               = HAL_I2C_STATE_READY;
07111     hi2c->Mode                = HAL_I2C_MODE_NONE;
07112     hi2c->ErrorCode           |= HAL_I2C_ERROR_AF;
07113 
07114     /* Process Unlocked */
07115     __HAL_UNLOCK(hi2c);
07116 
07117     return HAL_ERROR;
07118   }
07119   return HAL_OK;
07120 }
07121 
07122 /**
07123   * @brief  Convert I2Cx OTHER_xxx XferOptions to functionnal XferOptions.
07124   * @param  hi2c I2C handle.
07125   * @retval None
07126   */
07127 static void I2C_ConvertOtherXferOptions(I2C_HandleTypeDef *hi2c)
07128 {
07129   /* if user set XferOptions to I2C_OTHER_FRAME            */
07130   /* it request implicitly to generate a restart condition */
07131   /* set XferOptions to I2C_FIRST_FRAME                    */
07132   if (hi2c->XferOptions == I2C_OTHER_FRAME)
07133   {
07134     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_FIRST_FRAME;
07135   }
07136   /* else if user set XferOptions to I2C_OTHER_AND_LAST_FRAME */
07137   /* it request implicitly to generate a restart condition    */
07138   /* then generate a stop condition at the end of transfer    */
07139   /* set XferOptions to I2C_FIRST_AND_LAST_FRAME              */
07140   else if (hi2c->XferOptions == I2C_OTHER_AND_LAST_FRAME)
07141   {
07142     hi2c->XferOptions = I2C_FIRST_AND_LAST_FRAME;
07143   }
07144   else
07145   {
07146     /* Nothing to do */
07147   }
07148 }
